Pang Bingxun and Others Advise Sun to Refrain from Extreme Actions

A telegram to Sun was sent after being reviewed by He Yingqin.

If Sun obeys the order and leaves the army, his movements will be at his own discretion.

Wang Jingguo's Troops Fully Arrive at Linhe; No Changes in the Battle Situation in Ningxia

(Beiping) After Xu Fu came to Beiping, he had concrete results regarding the military actions against Sun, and the Jin-Sui troops are concentrating on the Linhe front. Six regiments of infantry and cavalry have arrived. Because Fu has completed the negotiations in Beiping, he is scheduled to return to Sui in the next day or two and go to Hetao to supervise the army. Pang Bingxun, Ji Yiqiao, and Hu Yukun believe that the people of the Northwest will suffer if the military actions are carried out, and if Sun's troops collapse in the future, they will harass everywhere. They sent a telegram to Sun in their private names, as a final piece of advice. The telegram was drafted yesterday and submitted to He for approval and was sent this morning. The content is divided into three points, advising Sun to immediately obey the order of the Military Affairs Commission to leave the army, and the troops are to be commanded by Yu Shiming, Ding Futing, and Liu Yueting to implement thorough downsizing. After Sun leaves the army, his personal safety will be guaranteed, and he will be free to live wherever he wants. If Sun's troops can obey the order to reorganize, there will be a way to provide all the military pay and rations, so there is no need to worry. (19th Special Telegram)

Jin Zunhua Telegrams to Advise Sun to Withdraw

(Beiping) After Pang Bingxun and others telegraphed Sun Dianying to leave the army and reorganize his troops, if Sun can sincerely accept this, the Military Affairs Commission can select three people to go to the front to supervise the troop withdrawal and downsizing. In the future, He Yingqin intends to take on part of Sun's living expenses. Jin Zunhua visited Fu Zuoyi last night, and they talked for about an hour. Jin telegraphed Sun today, in addition to conveying all the Beiping decisions, and advised Sun to withdraw immediately, so as not to betray the great love and desire for peace of all friends in Beiping. Whether Sun is sincere depends on whether he replies to the telegram. Wang Jingguo's entire force has arrived at Linhe. After Feng Yuxi's troops arrive at Datong, a part of the front line has also arrived. Zhao Chengshou's cavalry is moving from Pingdiquan towards Linhe. Fu's 73rd Division and Zhou Dai's two artillery regiments are advancing from their original defenses in order. (19th Special Telegram)

Rumor: Liu Yueting Has Been Dismissed by Sun

(Beiping) Military news, Ningxia telegram, the battle situation in Ningyuan has not changed. On the morning of the 17th, the cavalry brigade of our [illegible] division under Ma Zhongyi, and the cavalry of the 15th Route Army under Ma Guangzong, captured twenty staff officers and more than forty infantry and cavalry messengers sent by Sun Dianying to investigate the situation near Liangqu, about twenty-five miles north of Xincheng, along with more than thirty large and small guns and eight horses. Because of repeated failures, Sun has dismissed the pseudo-Front Commander Liu Yueting. Sun himself is now in the area of ​​the Great and Small Mosques, etc. (19th Special Telegram)

Sun Secretly Sends Representatives to Hong Kong and Guangdong

(Beiping) According to related sources, Sun Dianying, feeling that his end is near and he cannot survive, secretly sent representatives to Hong Kong and Guangdong to seek help, hoping to make a final attempt. However, Sun's character is known to the whole country, especially his disobedience to orders and westward invasion this time, and he has been abandoned by everyone. Hong Kong and Guangdong will not be fooled by him. Sun's move is a waste of effort. (19th Central News Agency Telegram)

Central Aircraft Distributes Leaflets

(Beiping) Two central aircraft flew to Ningxia, scattering a letter of advice to all officers and soldiers of the 41st Army, offering 30 yuan for each surrendered rifle, and those who wish to remain in the army will be employed at their original rank. (19th Special Telegram)

Jin-Sui Preparing for Military Actions Against Sun

(Taiyuan) Military agencies are actively preparing for Jin-Sui's dispatch of troops to attack Sun. Beiping has been in frequent communication with Yan by telegram, and concrete decisions will be made after Xu Yongchang and Fu Zuoyi return. (19th Special Telegram)

The Righteous Army Achieves a Great Victory in Attacking the Puppets

It is rumored that the Japanese army will be dispatched.

A major battle is expected soon.

(Nanjing) Special dispatch from Korea: Deng Tiemei, the commander of the Righteous Army, recently gathered his subordinates and raised the banner of anti-puppet in the triangular area of ​​Fengcheng, Andong, and Xiuyan counties, which is very popular with the people. The Japanese and puppet troops believe that they cannot resist and the momentum is even greater. There is a tendency to peek into the vicinity of Dongfengcheng, and the puppet side is very afraid. At the end of last month, Wang Dianzhong, the puppet Liaoning River area garrison commander, was sent by Yingkou to lead a large team of puppet troops to resist. On the 25th, they fought at Longwang Temple. The puppet army was defeated, with heavy casualties and loss of equipment. Wang sent a flying telegram for help. It is rumored that the Japanese army will be dispatched, and a major battle is expected soon. (19th Central News Agency Telegram)

Japanese Army Builds Airfields All Over the Four Northeastern Provinces

Thirty-eight have been completed.

(Beiping) The Japanese army has built 38 airfields in the Northeast in the past two years, and three are in the planning stage. Two have been completed in Fengtian and Harbin; one each in Dalian, Jinzhou, Lianshan Station, Taonan, Tongliao, Yuguan, Shanchengzhen, Zhuhezhen, Fangzheng County, Jiamusi, Fujin County, Ningguta, Muling County, Mishan County, Longjing Village, Jilin Provincial Capital, Dunhua, Changchun, Yanqing, Manzhouli, Hailar, Qiqihar, Keshan County, Longzhen, Nehe, Nenjiang, Daheihe, Mulan, Suihua, Chaoyang, Lingyuan, Chengde, Chicheng, Xinglong, Guyuan County, and Daheihe. The planned ones are one each in Bei'anzhen, Wuchang County, and Linxi. (19th Special Telegram)

Gubeikou Will Be Received at the End of the Month

The ceremony is the same as the reception of Yuguan.

The local Japanese army will postpone its withdrawal.

Yin Rugeng telegraphed Matsui yesterday for final negotiations.

(Beiping) Regarding the reception of Gubeikou, after negotiations between Yin Rugeng and the Japanese side, all arrangements have been agreed upon, and the reception will be implemented on the 28th of this month. The ceremony is roughly the same as the reception of Yuguan. Matsui, the deputy chief of the Chengde Special Affairs Agency, was sent by the Japanese side to be responsible for the handover. Yin telegraphed Matsui again this morning for final consultations, and a reply can be received tomorrow, which is generally not a problem. Yin is scheduled to travel to Gubeikou from Beiping on the morning of the 25th with Liu Youxun, director of the Gubeikou Affairs Bureau, Huo Shi, director of the Jizhou-Miyun Special Office, Wei Yonghe, captain of the first detachment of the War Zone Public Security First Team, and Qiu Haoting, the magistrate of Miyun County, to handle the matter. The original Japanese troops stationed in the port and various Japanese and puppet agencies cannot be withdrawn for the time being because there are no suitable houses outside. Other administrative and security matters will be completely handed over to our side for takeover. Malang will have to wait until the Gubeikou reception is completed before proceeding. (19th Special Telegram)

(Beiping) Qiu Haoting, the new magistrate of Miyun County, arrived in the county on the 16th and took office on the afternoon of the 17th. (19th Special Telegram)

Tax Cards in the Luanyu Area are Expected to be Recovered Soon

Tao Shangming is negotiating with the Japanese.

(Beiping) Tao Shangming said that since the reception of Yuguan, all the post-war matters and administrative plans have been actively promoted in accordance with the plan instructed by the authorities, and considerable results have been achieved in a short period of time. The cards along the Great Wall in Yuguan and Luanyu area are under negotiation and can be recovered independently soon. Our Yuguan Telegraph Bureau is still occupied by the Japanese side, and we also intend to negotiate and recover it soon. I will return to Tangshan in two or three days. (19th Special Telegram)

(Beiping) Yu Xuezhong said that after the reception of Yuguan, the police of the local Public Security Bureau have not yet restored their arms. Tao Shangming is negotiating with the Japanese side and it may be possible. The Baifengxiang cavalry division has advanced to Huaiqing to pursue and suppress Liu's bandits and can be demobilized soon. (19th Special Telegram)

Central and National Government Hold Memorial Week

(Nanjing) The Central Committee held its 118th Memorial Week at 9:00 a.m. on the 19th. Members Zhu Jiqing, Wang Luyi, Wang Qi, and all staff members, totaling more than 400 people, attended. Zhu Jiqing chaired the meeting and reported on the recent situation in the Northeast and the Far East international situation. The meeting was adjourned at 10:00 a.m. (19th Central News Agency Telegram)

(Nanjing) The National Government held Memorial Week at 10:00 a.m. on the 19th. Zhang Ji, Zhu Jiahua, Li Yuanding, He Yaozu, Cao Haosen, Zhang Daofan, Lu Chao, Wei Huai, Chen Qicai, and more than 400 staff members of the National Government attended. Chairman Lin led the ceremony. Ju Zheng reported, titled Two Contradictory Phenomena, generally meaning that the abolition of calendar year festivals has made merchants happy, as if it were a peaceful world, but the domestic industry and commerce are declining, shops are closing down one after another, and the countryside is bankrupt. According to statistics from the Ministry of Finance, food accounts for more than 270 million of the 1.3 billion yuan of imports. The situation is critical. To save the country and survive, the only way is to implement production and construction. (19th Central News Agency Telegram)

Mongol Immigration Vice-League Chief A Wang Arrives in Beiping

(Beiping) A Wang, the vice-league chief of Mongolian immigrants, was escorted to Beiping by Wang Jingguo on the 18th. This morning, he met with Fu Zuoyi and talked for half an hour. A Wang is scheduled to go to Beijing this week to negotiate Mongolian affairs. (19th Special Telegram)

President Wang Reports on Production and Construction at the Executive Yuan's Weekly Memorial Service

(Nanjing) The Executive Yuan held a weekly memorial service on the morning of the 19th, attended by all staff members. President Wang Zhaoming reported on production and construction as the direction of future efforts, roughly stating: On the 11th, he and Chairman Chiang issued a joint telegram, reiterating the main points of saving the country and surviving, emphasizing that the most urgent thing for treating the symptoms is to eliminate the communist bandits, and the most urgent thing for treating the root cause is production and construction. In the National Government's Memorial Week, he stated his purpose: In the past year of bandit suppression, Chairman Chiang personally supervised the war in Nanchang, and the proper dispatch and the use of the soldiers' lives have made considerable progress. In addition to the strategic superiority and tactical agility, the construction of blockhouses and the opening of highways are also important reasons for its victory. Following this trend, perseverance, dare to believe that the elimination of communist bandits, will be sure to have a grasp. As for production and construction, not only need talents, but also need material resources. In view of China's backward economic situation, there are many domestic production projects that should be constructed, but few can be implemented, which inevitably makes people discouraged, and even doubt that the so-called production and construction is just empty talk. At present, all agencies in the country only have maintenance fees, and no construction fees. During the period of bandit suppression, even the construction fees of the army have not been settled, so it is too early to be optimistic about the future of production and construction. However, enriching the people's strength and developing the national strength are the only way for production and construction. We must plan and proceed in the midst of great difficulties. Even if there is no large-scale, at least we must start from small things. If we cannot implement new plans, at least we must rectify the old ones. If we cannot seek development from the active aspect, at least we must eliminate the accumulated ills from the passive aspect. We hope to accumulate small amounts into many through continuous efforts. We dare not say how many construction projects have been successful in the past two years, but we have always held this determination to be responsible for production and construction and to do our work. Now, let's take the railway and transportation as examples to illustrate that production and construction is a real effort, a fact that has been worked hard in the past, and a direction that needs to be worked hard in the future. It is by no means just a propaganda slogan. First, let's talk about the railway. The railway is the lifeline of national transportation. Therefore, in the past two years, the government has focused on this work, one is to rectify the old roads, and the other is to build new roads. The most important ones that have been built one after another include: First, the Yuehan Line, which has never been connected from Liangguang to the Yangtze River since the 23rd year of the Republic of China, will start construction today and is expected to be completed within three years. Second, the Longhai Line, which connects Shaanxi and Gansu, is expected to reach Xi'an around the Double Ten Festival this year. Third, the Zhejiang-Jiangxi-Hunan Line, which connects the upper and lower reaches of the Yangtze River, is completely newly built. If the Yuehan Line is completed, there will be a direct trunk line in the central north and south; if the Longhai Line is completed, the northwest will have the possibility of development; if the Zhejiang-Jiangxi-Hunan Line is completed, the close connection of the economy and culture of the southeastern provinces will be more convenient. In addition, there are many others such as the construction of Laoyao Wharf on the Longhai Line, the repair of the Shanghai North Station on the Beijing-Shanghai Line, the completion of the Capital Ferry Project, the completion of the Hangzhou-Jiangxi Railway in Zhejiang Province, and others operated by private enterprises. It should be noted here that the construction of railways requires huge sums of money. In economically backward countries, these huge sums of money can only be raised from countries with abundant capital. Since we want to attract foreign investment, we must clearly indicate its guarantee for future investment. Therefore, the government attaches great importance to railway credit. Under certain conditions, the government is very willing to cooperate with foreign capital and is willing to do its best to maintain credit and protect the interests of investors. The government is determined to reorganize the previous railway debts owed to foreigners in a way that maintains the interests of both parties. In the past two years, considerable reorganization and repayment methods have been established for various railway debts, both Chinese and foreign. The debts of the national railways are roughly divided into (1) contract loans, (2) material loans, and (3) short-term loans. Regarding the first type, considerable repayment methods have been established for the accumulated debts of the Jinpu, Beijing-Shanghai, Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo, Daoqing, and Bianluo railways, and they are being implemented one after another. The debts of the Beining Railway are all performed in accordance with the contract. Regarding the second type, the material debts of the railways in the past two years, which have been reorganized and have repayment methods, include debts to merchants in the United Kingdom and the United States, totaling 100 million yuan. The third type of short-term loans is mostly owed to domestic banks, and considerable repayment methods have also been established and are being implemented one after another. Foreign creditors often complain about China's railways for failing to repay the debts and interest on time. The government naturally expresses its apology for the debts owed, but there are two points that it hopes creditors will pay attention to. One, railway creditors must know that due to the impact of the temporary situation, the debts have been delayed, which is a common occurrence in all countries. There are many reasons for the poor financial situation of Chinese railways, and it cannot all be blamed on one thing or one person. For example, before the construction of several railways was completed, the European War broke out suddenly, and the funds could not be continued to be raised in accordance with the contract, so the project was interrupted. However, the capital that has already been invested should still be planned year by year. The financial situation of the railway fell into extreme difficulties. The reason for this is the outbreak of the European War. Neither creditors nor the Chinese government can be blamed. Another example is the drop in the world's silver price and the recent global economic downturn, which has led to an increase in China's railway debt on the one hand and a decrease in revenue on the other, which is no different from a natural disaster. No country can stop it, and China cannot be blamed alone. Second, railway creditors must know that the Chinese government is not defaulting on its debts, but the premise for clearing debts is the reorganization and revitalization of the railway. If the railway is reorganized and revitalized, and the revenue increases, the interests of the creditors can be guaranteed. Therefore, to reorganize the railway and repay the debts, it is necessary for the creditors and the Chinese government to cooperate sincerely. Next, let's talk about transportation. The most important transportation industries are post, telecommunications, and aviation. In recent years, civil aviation has also become one of the transportation industries. As far as postal services are concerned, China has been running modern postal services for more than 60 years. Its scale and system are very developed and it has annual surpluses. However, in recent years, due to floods and banditry, and the Northeast Incident, the postal economy has suffered a huge loss of 10 million yuan. The internal business has also gradually deteriorated. In recent years, the government has devoted itself to the reorganization of the postal service itself and the development of the savings and remittance business. With the current economic situation, to reorganize the postal service itself, we can only adopt a policy of austerity, save expenses, and expand business. According to the report of the Ministry of Communications, as of the end of June last year, there were more than 12,000 post offices and more than 32,000 postal counters and agencies nationwide, with a postal route of 490,000 kilometers. This year, we will actively carry out additional installations, and it is expected that at least 5% of the postal route will be extended in another half year, and it will be extended to the border areas. As for the development of savings and remittance, we will focus on protecting the interests of depositors. Therefore, the government has decided to change the savings and remittances to the postal service, but still maintain its professional advantages, accounting independence, and not mixing it with the postal accounts. At the same time, a supervision system will be set up so that the people can openly supervise it. The investment restrictions are very strict. Although all the regulations have yet to be passed by the Legislative Yuan, they have gradually been implemented in fact. As far as telecommunications is concerned, the reorganization and development of telecommunications in the past year is divided into international telecommunications and domestic telecommunications. In the past, international telecommunications relied entirely on the submarine cables operated by foreign companies for communication. Since the completion of the Zhenru International Radio Station, China has successively communicated directly with the United States, France, Germany, Switzerland, and Manila, Java, Saigon, and Hong Kong via radio. On the one hand, it revised the contract with the Great Eastern, Great Northern, and Pacific companies for operating submarine cables in China to recover the right to send and receive telegrams; on the other hand, it added Sino-American circuits and opened Sino-Russian circuits. For direct communication with the United Kingdom, another Central Radio Station was specially added outside the Zhenru International Radio Station for special use due to the prosperity of commerce between the two countries. In addition, an international interchange station with the same scale as the Zhenru Radio Station was set up in Luoyang, and it is currently under construction and will be completed soon. As for domestic communication, in terms of wired communication, because of frequent years of war, banditry, and wind disasters, there has been a lot of damage. In the past year, a total of more than 5,000 miles of poles and lines have been repaired. The most important of these is the Hanyu Line, which is 2,500 miles long and is an important way for communication between central China and Sichuan and Tibet. It will be completed soon. In addition, the old-fashioned telegraph machines in various places will be replaced with new machines. More than 50 places have been completed in the past year. In terms of wireless communication, wireless communication was set up in important cities in the past. In the past year, the focus has been on the connection with the border areas. The plan to establish border radio stations has been determined. The two stations that have been established for communication this year are Xi'an and Zhangjia, one is to develop telecommunications and transportation in the northwest, and the other is to maintain contact between Mongolia and the central government. As for Xinjiang and Ximeng, it was originally planned to set up eight stations each, and everything has been prepared. Unfortunately, the local situation is unstable and it has been temporarily suspended. Other places such as Chahar, Suiyuan, Shaanxi, Gansu, Qinghai, Ningxia, and Sichuan and Kang have either been installed or are under planning and can be realized within a year. In terms of telephone, in the past year, the focus has been on the connection between long-distance telephones and urban telephones. The development plans that have been prepared are the three major trunk lines of Beijing-Hankou, Beijing-Tianjin, and Beijing-Hangzhou. The lines that are about to be built are the Beijing-Shanghai along the highway. The lines that have been completed are the Nanfu Line and the Ping-Chahar Line, and the telephone has been opened in six provinces of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Henan, Shandong, and Hebei, using telegraph poles and lines, which has reached more than 300 places. Recently, it is planned to set up a telephone network in the whole province of Jiangsu, and the first phase has started. As for the telephone in Beijing, the ones that have been improved and expanded in the past year include seven cities: Shanghai, Hankou, Tianjin, Qingdao, Suzhou, Zhengzhou, and Zhenjiang. Shanghai has the best results. In addition, wireless telephones are used to improve transportation. Domestic communication will be held in Beijing, Hankou, Fuzhou, and other places first. As for international telephones, the equipment has also been installed, and it will be opened as soon as the trial is successful. In terms of maritime administration, it is a great shame for China. Whether it is inland rivers or outer seas, they are all contracted by foreigners. Our only foundation is the two shipyards of Jiangnan and Mawei, and a China Merchants Bureau. The two shipyards of Jiangnan and Mawei are not large in scale, and the China Merchants Bureau has gone bankrupt due to poor management. Other private shipping industries are even more immature. Maritime administration construction requires huge expenses, and each ship costs hundreds of millions of gold. The government can only take the China Merchants Bureau back into state-owned management first and engage in rectification. In the past year, in addition to recovering almost all of the bureau's stocks, a debt clearing committee has been established, and the business has been actively reformed. The operating income in the first half of the year alone has reached 3.66 million yuan. As for civil aviation, it is operated by China and Eurasia Airlines. Before the development of China Airlines, the routes only included Shanghai-Hankou and Shanghai-Beiping. In the past year, the Shanghai-Hankou route has been actively developed and has been expanded to Chengdu. The Shanghai-Beiping line, which was previously suspended, has been changed to a coastal route. In addition, a coastal Shanghai-Guangdong line has been added, and the business is very developed. Recently, we have started to expand the route from Chengdu and connect Guiyang, Kunming, and other places, and have conducted a trial flight once. The Eurasia route of Eurasia Airlines is from Shanghai to Tacheng, and is connected to the Soviet Russian route in Tacheng, via Moscow to Berlin. Shanghai to Dihua was opened for several months, but it was interrupted again due to the unrest in the political situation in Xinjiang. Now it only goes to Lanzhou, and we are still continuing to find ways to restore it. In addition, Eurasia Airlines has added branch lines, one from Lanzhou to Xining and Ningxia, one from Dihua to Yili, and one from Dihua to Tashkent. The section from Xi'an to Beiping has been opened. Recently, a line from Guangzhou via Hankou to Xi'an has been added. The Guangdong-Hankou section has been successfully tested, and it can be opened as soon as the Guangzhou airport is completed. The above only mentions the four major industries of post, telecommunications, aviation, and civil aviation. The government has paid great attention to the reorganization of the agencies of these industries in the past year, with the aim of merging the telecommunications agencies and integrating the unevenly organized agencies of telegraph, telecommunications, wired telecommunications, and wireless telecommunications into a systematic organization. Secondly, accounting is reorganized, and active measures are taken to apply the new accounting system to the four industries. In addition to formulating various accounting systems, Chinese and foreign accountants are hired to audit each agency to make their accounts public. Those that have been implemented include Eurasia and China Airlines, and other agencies will also start to be held separately. Thirdly, personnel and business are reorganized. In the postal service, the personnel system is made more reasonable; in the telecommunications service, redundant personnel are laid off and work efficiency is reduced. In addition, the electricity fee is reduced to facilitate the people and promote business. In short, the government has reorganized the four industries of post, telecommunications, and aviation in the past year. There are many difficulties, and we can only continue to work hard to accomplish our work without slackening. The above briefly mentions the construction work in the two aspects of railway and transportation. From this, it can be seen that the so-called production and construction is not a propaganda, but a real effort to do. In the future, we can only gather the national strength and move forward. As for the diplomatic aspect, some people have criticized the government for being weak and incompetent. The government does not answer at all, because these criticisms, if they are out of enthusiastic criticism, the government cannot bear to answer, if they are out of malicious slander, the government does not bother to answer. To correct this weakness and incompetence, we can only enrich the people's strength and develop the national strength. The only way is to work hard on production and construction. As far as resisting strong neighbors is concerned, this is the only way. All the illusory psychology and fluke expectations that China used to have should be completely swept away. As far as maintaining international sympathy is concerned, this is also the only way. Someone asked me, what kind of diplomatic policy should China adopt today? I resolutely replied, improving internal affairs is the diplomatic policy that China should adopt today, because only by improving internal affairs can we make people look up to us and make people willing to be friends with us. Other than that, coalition and alliance are self-defeating. Therefore, we believe that diplomacy is only one aspect of internal affairs. Only by striving for achievement in internal affairs can we get rid of the predicament of weakness and incompetence in diplomacy. The reason why we issued a sincere telegram this month after last year's frugal telegram is nothing more than this. (19th Central News Agency Telegram)

Guangdong Army Withdraws from Longyan

Huang's division retreats to Shanghang and Wuping.

Only local militia remain in Longyan to guard the city.

Deng and Li's divisions also return to Guangdong for defense.

(Xiamen) Zhangzhou News: Huang Renhuan's division and Zeng's two brigades of the Guangdong Army in Longyan withdrew from Longyan on the 18th and retreated to Shanghang and Wuping, leaving only local militia to guard the city. All circles in Longyan telegraphed the Central Army, requesting that troops be sent to take over the defense. More than 2,000 remnants of the 19th Route Army, who had been reorganized, had previously retreated from Da Xiaochi to Yongding and entered Guangdong Province. After Mao Weishou transported the Seventh Route Army to Beijing, he came to Xiamen from Quanzhou on the 16th to wait for a boat to Ganzhou to meet Chiang. (19th Special Telegram)

(Hong Kong) Deng Longguang and Li Zhenliang's two divisions were ordered by Chen Jitang to return to their original defenses from the Fujian border. Wang Hechun's brigade was transferred to Xingning Meixian for training, and the remaining troops stationed in Fujian remained. (19th Special Telegram)

Current Commentary

A Perspective on the Inside Story of the Austrian Crisis

The recent riot of the Austrian Social Democratic Party arrived suddenly like a violent storm, catching people off guard. However, it suffered a crushing defeat within days. It seemed that Dollfuss' iron fist was able to control this precarious situation. Unexpectedly, as the Austrian government was celebrating its victory, news came that Dollfuss was seeking help from the League of Nations. This was followed by France, Italy, and Britain expressing their support for Austrian independence, as if the future disaster would be far worse than the current riot. This is truly perplexing.

However, upon examining the inside story, it becomes clear that Dollfuss's fears are not about the resurgence of the Social Democratic Party, but about the German National Socialist Party taking advantage of the chaos. What frightens France and Italy is not the Social Democratic Party's comeback, but the promotion of the German-Austrian merger, which would break the balance of power in the Danube region and restore Germany as the hegemon of Central Europe. According to the Treaty of Versailles, after the establishment of the peace treaty, Germany lost 27,000 square English miles of land in Europe and more than 6 million people, which were incorporated into France, Belgium, Italy, the Netherlands, Poland, and other countries. If the plan for the German-Austrian merger could be realized, Germany could suddenly increase its land by 32,000 English miles and its population by 6.5 million, instantly making up for its post-war losses in Europe. Wouldn't this be a joyous event? Germany and Austria share the same language and culture, and it is perfectly natural to merge and govern based on the principle of national self-determination. This cannot be equated with aggression and annexation. This is what those who understand the history of the German and Austrian nations have long known. The Treaty of Saint-Germain specifically stipulates the independence of Austria, also because the German and Austrian nations are the same, making it easy to merge. Therefore, this provision was specifically set up as a hidden danger, as a basis for future implementation of the ban. However, since the Great War, Germany and Austria have indeed had the desire to merge. For example, the Austrian draft constitution of December 12, 1918, declared, "German Austria is a part of the German Republic. Special laws will be enacted separately regarding the participation of German Austria in the legislative and administrative affairs of the German Republic and the implementation of German laws in Austria." The following year, the official Austrian constitution also contained similar statements. As for the German constitution, although there is no explicit expression, Article 2 states, "For the purpose of exercising the right of national self-determination, Germany may accept the merger of other countries." The intention is self-evident. In the spring of 1921, the majority of the Austrian people advocated resolving the issue of German-Austrian merger through voting, but unfortunately, they were suppressed by external forces and failed. After that, the German-Austrian merger almost became an illusion. It was not until after 1928 that another path was sought, from an economic alliance to a political union. Unexpectedly, France saw through the hidden motive and pointed out that it violated the treaty. Finally, in 1931, the dream of this economic alliance was shattered by the decision of the International Court of Justice. Since then, the German-Austrian merger has fallen into a stalemate again. It was not until after the rise of Hitler, the leader of the German National Socialist Party, that there was a turning point. Hitler himself was of Austrian origin, and his desire for merger was even stronger than others. The means he adopted were also very clever, that is, organizing the same National Socialist Party in Austria, seizing its political power, and manipulating its cabinet, so that Austria's domestic and foreign policies would be entirely at the mercy of Germany. In this way, it would not conflict with the provisions of the treaty, and it could achieve the actual effect of the merger. Therefore, Hitler believed that this was the best plan.

However, Hitler's method, clever as it is, has encountered more difficulties than before. In the past, the opposition to the German-Austrian merger came mostly from external forces, but now even Austria holds different views. The reason is that Hitler's administration is reckless and radical, favoring his own party and excluding dissidents. Once he came to power, he had no one but himself, which frightened the Austrian political parties. In the past, they sought merger but could not obtain it, but now they regard merger as a suicidal path. In the past two years, Dollfuss has spared no effort to restrict the activities of the Nazi Party in Austria, all driven by this terror. Eliminating dissidents is originally what the Nazi Party excels at, but now Dollfuss is using the other person's methods to treat the other person, and as a result, he has also unconsciously become fascist. In short, in this incident, the Austrian Social Democratic Party was the first to bear the brunt, but in terms of its international seriousness, the Nazi Party's activities are the root cause. Otherwise, Dollfuss and countries such as France and Italy would not need to be so alarmed. If you don't believe me, look at the division of Austrian political parties today. The ruling party is the Christian Social Party, whose backbone is conservative Catholics who have never advocated the German-Austrian merger. The Social Democratic Party, on the other hand, mostly leans towards merger. Therefore, it is only reasonable to say that the Social Democratic Party's activities are secretly assisted by the Nazi Party.

I still remember that before Hitler came to power, his slogans and catchphrases were so beautiful that it seemed as if Germany would have a way out once he took office. Unexpectedly, it has been nearly two years since he came to power, and many of the promises he made to the German people have not been fulfilled. Now, the international situation is even more unfavorable to him. Even Austria, which shares the same language and culture, has turned against him and would rather seek protection from foreign countries. For Hitler, I really don't know what other tricks he has to clean up the mess.

The Diet is Tense over the Review of the Bribery Case of the Minister of Education

Agreement on a Reward of Two Million Yen

Newspapers Wrapped Five Hundred Thousand Yen in Hundred-Yen Notes

Okamoto Claims to Have Obtained Various Evidence

(Tokyo) The inquiry committee, which the entire nation of Japan is watching, convened at 10:40 this morning. Today's meeting summoned Okamoto and Eto to deliberate on the 50,000 yen bribery case involving Education Minister Hatoyama and the Sakhalin Industries Company, as well as the disciplinary problems related to the Japanese Artificial Silk Company and Kobe Steel Company, which involved 120 Diet members from the Seiyukai party. The atmosphere in the Diet was extremely tense. Committee Chairman Shimada first reported that the committee had requested the attendance of various ministers and secretaries Lin and Yoneda, according to the decision of the previous meeting.

The inquiry began immediately. Hamada Kunimatsu asked,

I have heard that Mr. Okamoto has evidence to prove the truth of this case. Is this true?

Okamoto replied,

Of course, I have a factual basis before I dare to speak. I can reveal the names of the people involved in this case, but there will be those who will suffer as a result. Who should bear the responsibility for this must be decided first.

Okamoto and Hamada answered each other several times. Okamoto wanted to explain the truth about Education Minister Hatoyama's trip to Kansai to resolve the Kyoto Imperial University Prof. Kawakami incident, during which he secretly engaged in activities related to the Japanese Artificial Silk and Kobe Steel Company problems. Committee Chairman Shimada warned Okamoto,

Mr. Okamoto, what you want to say is not related to Mr. Hamada's questions. Please answer the questions.

At this time, Kiyose Ichiro of the Nationalist Alliance heckled Shimada from his seat,

Does the committee chairman want to collude with Mr. Hamada to prevent Okamoto from speaking?

A dispute arose between the two, and the Diet was temporarily disturbed.

Agreement on Two Million Yen Reward

Then, Okamoto continued,

This issue cannot be explained in a single sentence. When Education Minister Hatoyama stayed in Kansai, his secretary, Mr. Lin, met with Nomura Tokushichi, a giant in the financial world, to mediate the disposal of shares. An agreement on a reward of two million yen was reached between the two. Mr. Yoneda is also involved in this matter. I have brought the documentary evidence. If necessary, I can present it to the public.

Hamada asked,

Does Mr. Okamoto have any evidence regarding his statement on the 13th about the Sakhalin Industries Company?

Okamoto replied,

Before discussing the evidence issue, it is necessary to explain whose words have more probative value, Education Minister Hatoyama's or mine. Education Minister Hatoyama denies the fact that I met with the Hatoyama couple, which is unfounded.

Newspapers Wrapped Five Hundred Thousand Yen in Hundred-Yen Notes

Okamoto then mentioned the main points of the Sakhalin Industries issue, saying,

At that time, Mr. Hatoyama said to me, "Fujita Yoshisaburo is waiting. You can go and see him immediately." I went to see Fujita, and Fujita immediately said, "Are you handling this matter?" I asked, "What matter?" Then Fujita was very flustered. When I returned to Mr. Hatoyama's place, Hatoyama said to me, "We have agreed that you have received the money. So, when the court asks about this matter, please answer that you have indeed received 50,000 yen in hundred-yen notes wrapped in newspaper." I immediately said to Hatoyama, "If this case is related to the rise and fall of your family, then I can handle this matter for you on your behalf." Later, I was questioned by the judicial authorities for the crime of destroying evidence because of this issue, but the prosecution was suspended.

Hamada asked,

The point of suspended prosecution is very important. Is this a fact?

Okamoto replied,

I heard it said that way. I have not yet investigated whether it is true or false.

The meeting temporarily adjourned at 11:55.

The inquiry into Okamoto Ichi's case continued at 1:40 p.m. today in a tense atmosphere. Regarding the relationship between the Kobe Steel stock and the Taiwan Bank stock issues and the two ministers Hatoyama and Mitsuchi, Mr. Hamada asked,

Regarding the sale of Taiwan Bank stock, even if there were improprieties in terms of timing and value, the existence of a relationship between Yoneda and Lin is still a separate issue. Who manufactured the diagram that Mr. Okamoto claims to have obtained (which records the system of handing over money)?

Okamoto replied,

Mr. Kuba Yoshimichi, a member of the Seiyukai party.

Many of Those Implicated Choose to Remain Silent

Okamoto then handed the diagram to Committee Chairman Shimada. The committee chairman then handed it to the other members for them to pass around and view. Committee Chairman Shimada then stated,

This diagram will be copied and returned later.

Okamoto immediately said,

I don't want to cause useless harm. If I explain the inside story, then many people will be implicated. Therefore, it is better to remain silent.

Regarding Morita Masayoshi, the administrator of Hatoyama's farm in northern Korea, he transported many hundred-yen notes last year and was ordered by his master to distribute them. It is said that the number of people was over one hundred.

When Ueda wanted to pursue the matter further, Okamoto said, There is no need to answer this matter any further.

Next, Kiyose Ichiro asked why the Minister of Justice had requested the documents related to the Fujita Kozaaburo incident three days ago and had not yet submitted them.

What After the Collapse of the Saito Cabinet?

The Takahashi-Yamamoto Coalition Cabinet Theory

(Tokyo) After the deterioration of the disciplinary problems, the resignation of Education Minister Hatoyama has become unavoidable and is likely to develop into the resignation of the Saito Cabinet. According to observations in political circles, if the Saito Cabinet resigns due to the disciplinary problems, the Emperor's order to form a cabinet will definitely not be given to Saito again. Who will be the leader of the succeeding cabinet? It is predicted that Vice President of the Privy Council Hiranuma or Korean Governor-General Ugaki will step forward. There is also a theory of a coalition cabinet between Finance Minister Takahashi and Home Minister Yamamoto. This coalition cabinet has a major relationship with the establishment of the budget for the ninth fiscal year. After the fall of the Saito Cabinet, the only cabinet that has the possibility of temporarily cleaning up the political situation and ensuring the smooth establishment of the budget is this cabinet. Therefore, there is talk of such a coalition cabinet. (19th United Press Dispatch)

Minister of Justice Oyama replied,

There is absolutely no intention to refuse to submit the records of the public trial. Kiyose asked,

What is the meaning of "newspapers do not constitute a crime"?

Minister of Justice Oyama replied,

The records in the newspapers do not bear any responsibility.

Why Doesn't the Court Summon Okamoto, Who Received 50,000 Yen in Bribes?

Kiyose Hopes That the Minister of Justice Will Maintain a Strict Position

Next, Mr. Taketomi asked,

Why was Mr. Okamoto, who received 50,000 yen in bribes, not summoned to the prosecutor's office to conduct an investigation?

Minister of Justice Oyama replied,

At that time, there were many major incidents, and there was a backlog of cases. The so-called Fujita incident had not been reported to this office. The fact that he was not summoned can only be known after the submission of the investigation documents.

Next, Diet member Morita Masayoshi, a member of the inquiry committee, requested to speak,

I once managed Hatoyama's farm in Korea, but the world misunderstands this farm. You should know that this facility was intended to help the poor people of Korea. That was the purpose. There was no profit involved. I am not a rich man either. Mr. Hatoyama did not trust me. There is no such thing as Mr. Okamoto said about distributing huge sums of money.

Regarding the case of Kuba Yoshimichi, who allegedly created the diagram, Mr. Morita also claimed,

The Sixth High School Association is a gathering of graduates of the Sixth High School, including Mr. Lin and Mr. Yoneda. Mr. Kuboi is also a member of the association. The so-called diagram may be a temporary notebook entry, which cannot be the situation described by Mr. Okamoto. It should be requested that it be withdrawn.

Mr. Okamoto also spoke about Mr. Morita's claims, but it was extremely unclear. Finally, he raised various questions to Minister of Justice Oyama. The meeting adjourned at 4 p.m. (19th Japan United Press Dispatch)

Saito's Advance or Retreat is Difficult

Divergence of Opinions Within the Cabinet on the Issue of Total Resignation

(Tokyo) Regarding the disciplinary problems of Education Minister Hatoyama and others, the consensus of the top leaders of the government, including the Prime Minister, the Minister of Finance, and the Minister of Home Affairs, is as follows: (1) Regardless of the truth or falsehood of the matter, given that the situation has reached this point, it is hoped that Education Minister Hatoyama will voluntarily express his intention to resign. The position of the succeeding Minister of Education will not be filled temporarily, and the Prime Minister will concurrently assume the position. (2) If Education Minister Hatoyama has the determination to explain himself regarding the impeachment by the inquiry committee and the House of Peers, the government will not advise him to resign because the matter is different from the case of former Minister of Commerce Nakajima. Instead, it will support the Minister of Education to deal with the Diet. (3) Regarding the establishment of the budget for the next year, no matter how the House of Peers and the House of Representatives criticize it, we will endure it. Although the submission of the additional budget for the Ministry of Agriculture and Forestry has been delayed due to the illness of Minister of Agriculture and Forestry Goto, the preparations have been completed. If Minister of Agriculture and Forestry Goto's illness is prolonged and the political situation is strained, it will be submitted to the Cabinet Council in the absence of Minister of Agriculture and Forestry Goto and urgently submitted to the Diet. The approval of the Minister of Agriculture and Forestry will be requested afterward. However, many young cabinet members advocate for a total resignation at once because the investigation by the inquiry committee, if expanded, will affect not only Education Minister Hatoyama and Minister of Railways Mitsuchi, but also Minister of Justice Oyama, who was recently appointed Prosecutor-General, and Finance Minister Takahashi, who is responsible for supervising the disposal of shares owned by Taiwan Bank. Therefore, the earlier the time of total resignation, the better. Furthermore, it is difficult to expect a smooth transition of power in the future. Prime Minister Saito has the possibility of forming a cabinet again. Therefore, the opinion advocating for a total resignation is currently opposed by another opinion within the cabinet. (19th Den-tsu Dispatch)

If the Minister of Education Resigns, It Will Also Be Unfavorable for the Minister of Railways

The Political Situation is Extremely Serious

(Tokyo) The Japanese political situation is extremely serious due to the internal strife of the Seiyukai party and the disciplinary problems of Education Minister Hatoyama. The opinions of various parties in the political world on this situation are generally as follows:

(1) Whether Education Minister Hatoyama should take responsibility and resign will be considered when Hatoyama voluntarily decides to resign.

(2) After the Minister of Education resigns, it is expected that there will be no pursuit of the responsibility of the entire cabinet. However, it is quite obvious that the faction aiming to overthrow the cabinet will shift its attack target to Minister of Railways Mitsuchi. In that case, the cabinet will be busy considering the advancement and retreat of cabinet members, so it will be difficult to maintain the regime as before.

(3) However, the current cabinet has a major responsibility to strive to pass the budget bill through the Diet because of the "Manchukuo" issue and the extraordinary situation in 1935 and 1936. Furthermore, its important mission of stabilizing the people's hearts has not yet been accomplished. Therefore, arbitrarily abandoning the cabinet violates its own mission. If the resignation of the Minister of Education is realized, Prime Minister Saito will negotiate with Seiyukai President Suzuki and request him to recommend a successor. In the event that the Seiyukai cannot consider the successor issue due to the expansion of internal strife, the Prime Minister may temporarily serve concurrently as the Minister of Education to avoid a political upheaval and ensure the smooth establishment of the budget.

(4) However, since the attitudes of the inquiry committee and the House of Peers have not yet been determined, it is still difficult to predict. It is reported that the military's opinion still advocates the doctrine of putting national defense first, with the most urgent task being to pass the budget for the ninth fiscal year. If the budget cannot be established due to a political upheaval, the national defense work will be greatly affected. Therefore, regardless of whether the current cabinet falls or not, they hope that the budget will be established. (18th Japan United Press Dispatch)

(Tokyo) Education Minister Hatoyama visited Seiyukai President Suzuki yesterday for a short time to discuss the issue of his own advancement and retreat and the future political situation. After a long secret conversation, he told reporters after returning home that his visit to President Suzuki was naturally to discuss his personal issues. Londoners Still Observing

(London) Recently, the United States has been purchasing large quantities of silver in the London market, leading to a general belief that the U.S. government's silver policy is rapidly developing. However, Londoners are currently maintaining a wait-and-see attitude, awaiting a clear statement of the U.S.'s concrete policy. If the U.S. intends to adopt a silver policy similar to its gold policy, difficulties are bound to arise, as the world has a large silver reserve. According to the opinion of a leading broker in the precious metals industry, such action by the U.S. would be greatly detrimental to the Far East, resulting in a large concentration of silver in New York, thus reducing currency reserves and causing contraction. Furthermore, silver, being a commodity, is best left to rise with commodity prices, rather than artificially increasing its value. Silver mining stocks on the stock exchange have seen their market prices rise in anticipation of U.S. action. The foreign exchange market anticipates that the Bank of France's gold reserves will gradually flow into the U.S. as the dollar's value falls. France's current austerity plan may increase the difficulties of the German treasury, which may be forced to raise debt, thus defeating the purpose of austerity. (19th, Reuters)

The Remains of the Belgian King are Moved to the Palace, and the World Mourns in Unison

Heads of State Offer Condolences to the Belgian Royal Family

European Politicians Flock to Bear the Coffin

The Successor Will Ascend the Throne on the 23rd

Brussels Today, at dusk, the remains of the Belgian King were moved from the suburban Laeken Palace to the Royal Palace in the capital. The lights were extinguished on all streets passed. Retired soldiers lined the streets, holding torches high. When they reached the Tomb of the Unknown Soldier, they paused for one minute, and the whole group observed a moment of silence. (19th, Reuters)

Brussels The remains of the Belgian King will be moved from Laeken Palace to the capital on Sunday, and laid in state at the Royal Palace, with the funeral scheduled for Thursday. The new King, Leopold, will be sworn in on Friday. (18th, National Telegram)

Brussels Messages of condolence from all over the world are pouring in to the Royal Family, praising the late King's bravery and wisdom. President Roosevelt sent a telegram to the Belgian Queen, and Secretary of State Hull sent a telegram to the Belgian Foreign Minister to express his condolences.

After receiving the news of the Belgian King's death, British Foreign Secretary Simon personally announced it to the British public via radio and praised the Belgian King's achievements during his lifetime. According to reliable sources, British King George is likely to lead one of his sons to bear the coffin here. The British King personally telegraphed the Belgian Crown Prince to express his condolences, including the words "In the dark years of the European War, the King's bravery encouraged the Allied forces, and the British Empire will never forget it. Now, I wish to follow the Belgian people to mourn the deceased friend." In addition, British Crown Prince, German President Hindenburg, and Italian Prime Minister Mussolini all sent sincere telegrams of condolence. After hearing the news, Mussolini immediately ordered the entire country to fly flags at half-mast to express mourning.

The Paris Minister of Post and Telecommunications telegraphed all domestic radio stations to stop broadcasting for half an hour from 8 p.m. last night to express mourning, and ordered that the broadcasting programs in the next few days must be in line with the spirit of mourning until after the Belgian King's funeral. The French government has ordered a month of mourning for the Belgian King.

French Prime Minister Doumergue, accompanied by cabinet members Taittinger and Herriot, departed from Paris for Brussels today to express condolences. The French National Assembly suspended its morning session to express its mourning. The Speaker, despite his illness, attended the session, intending to have all members of the National Assembly stand to express the French Parliament's condolences for the death of the Belgian King.

According to news from the capital of Sweden, the Swedish Royal Family will observe three weeks of mourning. Crown Prince Gustav will come here to attend the funeral.

A Glimpse of the Belgian King's Remains

Dressed in the Uniform of an Army Lieutenant General, Holding a Cross

Brussels Tonight, Count de Lannoix, the master of ceremonies in the palace, and Aide-de-Camp de Thieusies met with representatives of the Belgian and foreign press in the Laeken Palace, granting them an audience with the Royal Spirit. They visited the King's office, seeing the desk piled high with books and magazines, some with open pages. The King's lifelong dedication to scholarship could be seen here. In the cloakroom, the clothes the King was wearing before the accident were still hanging on the wall. Entering the Royal bedroom, the King's remains were seen lying across the Royal bed, with bloodstains and bruises visible on his hands. In his hands, he held a small ivory cross, which was given to the King by the blacks of the Congo in 1928 when he visited Africa. In front of the bed was a table, on which was placed a large cross, two candlesticks, and a dish of holy water with a small branch of boxwood. The steel helmet, military cap, and gloves that the King wore in the trenches during the war were placed on the cupboard, and a military sword was placed on the bookshelf. The Royal Spirit is now guarded by Father Delannoy, the palace chaplain, and two nuns. Members of the diplomatic corps have come to pay their respects to the Spirit. The successor, Prince Leopold, arrived from Switzerland at midnight. The son-in-law, Italian Crown Prince Umberto, is scheduled to arrive here tomorrow. (18th, Havas)

Brussels The remains of the Belgian King are now laid in state at Laeken Palace, dressed in the uniform of an army lieutenant general, with the Grand Cross pinned to his chest, and covered in a shroud. His hands are holding an ivory cross, made by African blacks. When the King visited the Belgian Congo in 1928, a priest presented it to the King. The spiritual bed is covered with a purple blanket, with several white lilac flowers placed on it. In front of the spiritual bed is a table with white candles burning and a dish of holy water. Two royal doctors will meet with experts tonight to apply preservatives to the King's remains in preparation for the state funeral. One nurse, one priest, and two nuns will guard the spiritual bed all night, chanting scriptures. (19th, Reuters)

Official Investigation of the Cause of the Disaster

Climbing the Summit, Loose Rocks Cause Him to Fall

Brussels According to the official report of the judicial investigation into the death of Belgian King Albert I, the King's attendants rushed to the location the King had told them to go to at 5 p.m. They did not see the King and searched everywhere without finding him. At 7 p.m., they called the local gendarmerie and the palace from a nearby coffee shop. Aide-de-Camp de Thieusies, Royal Physician Nolf, and Count Segluna, upon hearing the news, rushed to the scene and searched separately. Because of the dense fog, the search was quite difficult. Later, they found traces of the King climbing the mountain. It was not until 2 a.m. that they discovered the King's remains. They immediately carried the remains into a car and transported them to Laeken Palace. Judicial officials arrived at the scene of the accident at 3:40 a.m. and conducted a joint investigation with various experts. By 8 a.m., they had determined that the King had climbed to the highest point of the mountain. They found the King's footprints there. At that time, the King was standing on a large rock. Unfortunately, the rock fell, and the King fell with it. His body touched the rocks and died instantly. The corpse continued to roll down the cliff until it stopped 50 meters below. The scarf, handbag, cap, belt, and military items he carried with him were scattered everywhere and have all been found. (18th, Havas)

Brussels An investigation of the site of the Belgian King's accident proved that the King had reached his destination that day. On the way back, the King climbed a dangerous cliff. Usually, one could climb by holding onto protruding rocks, but on this day, one of the rocks the King was holding onto suddenly came loose, causing the King to fall about 40 feet. Before he hit the ground, his head struck a rock and broke open. His body fell on its side, with its feet upward. There was a pool of blood around the head, and a part of the brain was on the rock. (19th, National Telegram)

Warsaw was officially recognized as the capital of the country in 1633, the year of the coronation of Władysław IV. (Chengdu) The Third and Fourth Route Armies for Suppressing Bandits began to attack Nanjiang, a strategic pass to Bazhong and the stronghold of Dingshan, on the 9th. Niu Huilin Returns to Shanghai

(Hangzhou) After waking up on the morning of the 19th, Weng Wenhao called his daughter to ask about household matters, and then had milk and other things. He had bowel movements once in the morning and once in the afternoon. Extradition Case of Assassin of Ma Zhanshan in the British Concession of Tianjin

Fugitive Hides in a Certain Country’s Concession

(Tianjin) The assassin who attempted to murder Ma Zhanshan was detained in the British Municipal Council, but he did not provide any real confession, not even revealing his name. The ringleader is surnamed Zhang, and there are many accomplices, all from Shandong province. Besides those arrested, the rest fled into a certain country's concession. The Public Security Bureau sent out numerous detectives to vigorously search for them. The arrested female assassin, surnamed Cao, is about thirty years old, with bound feet, dressed as a servant. When captured, three Mauser pistols and two hand grenades were found in her crotch. She struggled for a long time before being subdued. On the 18th night, due to the British Municipal Council's investigative efforts, she was extradited to our Public Security Bureau this afternoon. Ning Xiangnan, the Chief of the Public Security Bureau, rewarded the two special agent teams of the bureau with 200 yuan for their efforts in handling this case. Ma Zhanshan will also give a reward. This time, a certain country offered a reward of 100,000 for assassinating Ma. The traitorous assassins, after receiving orders, waited a long time for an opportunity to strike but could not find one. They even waited for many days at Zhang Jiang Yuanxing's bathhouse in the British concession, where Ma was expected to go, planning to attack him when he came out of the bath. However, they failed because Ma was ill. Every day, someone disguised as a rickshaw puller waited in front of Ma's residence, but they still could not find a chance to act. Finally, they planned to rent a house. The special agent team had been investigating this case for a month before taking action on the 18th. At that time, the team members were all dressed as rickshaw pullers or electricians. They suddenly attacked unexpectedly. Each assassin carried one or two handguns in their sleeves, and because of their quick movements, the assassins were unable to fight back. (19th Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) The individuals handed over to the Public Security Bureau by the British Municipal Council for the assassination attempt on Ma include: (1) Ma Dianchen, 33 years old, from Jiangsu province, former president of the Tianjin-Suzhou People's Hospital. He committed suicide out of fear of punishment and is now dead. (2) He Yuqing, 20 years old, from Jiangsu province. (3) Gao Li, 19 years old, from Henan province. (4) Xue Xiancai, 33 years old, from Shandong province. (5) Zheng Yufu, 26 years old, from Jiangsu province. (6) Wang Chengyun, 24 years old, from Shandong province. (19th Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) On the 19th, the Japanese military headquarters stationed in Tianjin sent two military officers to the Hebei Provincial Government, intending to protest that the assassination attempt on Ma Zhanshan was instigated by the other side.
