Dispersed Soldiers of the 19th Route Army Arrive in Guangdong for Repatriation

The old and weak are given travel expenses to return home.

The young and strong are added to various armies.

Guangzhou Correspondent: Besides the part of the 19th Route Army that was incorporated by the central government and the part that joined the Guangdong side in Longyan and was reorganized into the Independent 3rd Brigade, there is another part that was not incorporated by either side and voluntarily chose to retire and return to their hometowns. This unit, originally stationed in Quanzhou and Hui'an in Fujian, consists of scattered soldiers from the 61st Division, the 19th Route Army Training Regiment, the 130th Brigade, and the 5th Army Supplementary Division, totaling over 2,000 people. Led by administrator Ni Jianchu, they returned south from Xiamen with two teams of military police from the 19th Route Army (these two teams of military police were borrowed from Guangdong by the 19th Route Army years ago). On the 8th, they took advantage of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Xinfeng ship passing through Shantou. They landed in Shantou, and the Shantou Public Security Bureau sent a team to take care of them to maintain order, designating a place for them to temporarily stay. At the same time, the local charitable organization and Chamber of Commerce provided porridge for them. At 5:00 PM, the scattered soldiers returned to the ship and sailed to Guangzhou. On the morning of the 11th, the Xinfeng ship arrived at Huangpu waters in Guangzhou, where they landed and awaited repatriation. At around 7:00 PM, a small group of about a hundred people took a small boat to Guangzhou City, landing at the Tianzi Wharf, wandering around Yonghan South Road, Weixin Road, and the Bund area. The Provincial Public Security Bureau and Military Police Headquarters immediately sent a team to escort the hundred-odd scattered soldiers back to Huangpu. According to the scattered soldiers, most of them are from the West River and South Road districts of Guangdong Province. They previously belonged to Mao Weishou's unit of the 19th Route Army. They did not want to be reorganized this time, and the central government issued travel expenses of five or ten yuan, which has already been spent along the way. Although they have arrived in Guangzhou, they still have not been able to return to their hometowns, expressing unspeakable sadness. Later, the military police first sent the small group of scattered soldiers back to Huangpu for concentration, so that they could be repatriated. The next day, Chen Jitang immediately sent several staff officers and adjutants on electric boats to Huangpu to settle the scattered soldiers. The repatriation method was to first call the roll of each scattered soldier, ask them about their situation, and register them separately according to their age and health. Those who were old and weak were given ten yuan in travel expenses to return to their hometowns. Most of the young and strong were still willing to serve as soldiers, so their names were recorded in a roster, and they were assigned to fill vacancies in various armies according to their original positions. Chen Jitang ordered all army division and brigade commanders, and directors of rear affairs offices, to submit the number of vacancies in their units to the General Headquarters so that they could be selected and replenished. On the 13th, the rear personnel of various army divisions and brigades were sent to Huangpu to inspect and incorporate the soldiers and then send them to the front line to replenish the ranks. As for the supplementary soldiers under the First Army, they have been sent to Dayu to await distribution these past days. (February 15th)

Assassination of Former Chargé d'Affaires to Japan, Zhuang Jingke

The perpetrators were four thugs.

Zhuang was shot dead on the spot.

Speculation on important background.

Tianjin Correspondent: At 10:00 PM on Lunar New Year's Eve, Zhuang Jingke, the former chargé d'affaires to Japan, who resided at No. 29, the corner of Akashi Street North and Fukushima Street in the Japanese concession in Tianjin, was suddenly broken into by four thugs and shot dead. Because it was the Lunar New Year holiday, few people knew about this incident. It is reported that Zhuang Jingke, courtesy name Jinggao, was from Minhou, Fujian. He graduated from the law department of Waseda University in Japan and successively served as a councilor and secretary of the Governor's Office of the Three Eastern Provinces, secretary of the Ministry of the Army, judge of the Supreme Court, director of the Ministry of Justice, and first-class secretary and chargé d'affaires of the Embassy in Japan. During Duan Qirui's administration, he was also an important figure in the Anfu Clique. When Chu Yupu governed Zhili, he once served as a special envoy for foreign affairs in Tianjin. After Chu's defeat, Zhuang retired and lived at home. Because he had studied law, he practiced law in Tianjin, handling civil and criminal litigation, with no shortage of cases entrusted to him. In his free time, he would invite former Anfu Clique figures such as Minister of Justice Yao Zhen, Vice Minister of Transportation Yao Guozhen, and his relative Zhu Yujun, the former Director-General of Transportation, to his residence to chat or play mahjong. A few days before Lunar New Year's Eve, Zhuang suddenly instructed his servant that a Mr. Chen would visit him soon. If he was home at the time, there was no need to report it; he could be invited in directly, as he had a litigation case to discuss. At about 10:00 PM on Lunar New Year's Eve, the servant heard someone knocking on the door. He asked for the name of the visitor through the door, who answered that he was Mr. Chen, here to discuss a case. The servant remembered his master's instructions and opened the door to welcome the guest. At that time, four strong men stood outside the door, looking fierce. Seeing the door open, two of them turned into the house to guard the door, while the other two rushed upstairs. They seemed very familiar with the route and went straight to the guest room on the third floor. At this time, Zhuang heard that the guest had arrived and stood in the hall to greet him. He glanced at the two men entering the hall and realized that he did not know them. Just as he was about to ask, the two strong men drew their guns and opened fire on Zhuang, firing several shots in succession, hitting him twice in the chest, once in the left arm, and once in the right neck. Zhuang was immediately splattered with blood and fell to the ground. After committing the crime, the two men ran back downstairs, joined the two men guarding the door, turned to the street corner, got into a car, and fled. At the time of the shooting, families were celebrating the New Year, and the sound of firecrackers was deafening. Although some people nearby heard the noise, they thought it was firecrackers and did not pay attention. It was not until a few minutes after the thugs left that the servant reported it to the Japanese police at the street corner, who relayed it to the special operations team of the Japanese police station. They conducted a search, but the thugs were long gone. The next day, the court received notification from the Japanese police station and sent prosecutor Hu to investigate, fill out a coroner's report, and file a case for wanted suspects. The body was placed in a coffin by Zhuang's son, Kaiyong, and his relative, Zeng Yujun. The wake was held on the 14th, the funeral on the 15th, and the burial on the 16th. According to general speculation, Zhuang's murder certainly has an important background: (1) Zhuang recently accepted a case involving the divorce lawsuit of Zhang Zongchang's twenty-first concubine. Zhang's twenty-first concubine, named Fugui, originally came from a brothel. Before joining Zhang, she had a flag in Tianjin. After Zhang's death, she was unwilling to be lonely and lived with Zhang's bodyguard as if they were husband and wife. Recently, the two had a falling out and could not continue their relationship. Fugui feared that the bodyguard would be a rogue and would harass her after the separation, so she hired Zhuang to handle the lawsuit. Zhuang had been handling this case for many days, and it was about to succeed. The bodyguard was bound to lose, so people suspect that Zhuang's murder may be related to this. (2) Although Zhuang was a lawyer, he had studied in Japan and served as a diplomat in Japan and had many dealings with Japanese people. Recently, Puyi usurped the title of Emperor in the Northeast. The traitors in Tianjin were plotting to respond at the time or make other expressions. Zhuang was working hard to win over these people, and it was said that he had illegal plans. Therefore, his tragic death has some political background. (16th)

Xuzhou's Commercial Decline

丨Numerous Business Closures Across Various Sectors丨

Xuzhou dispatch: Since the past few years, the commercial situation in Xuzhou has been declining, reaching its lowest point now. The fifth day of the new lunar year is the time for businesses to take stock, clean up, and reopen, marking the start of a year's operations. In previous years, countless new ventures would emerge, but now, many businesses are closing down at this time. The societal bankruptcy is evident. Here's a sector-by-sector breakdown based on our investigations: (1) Banking and Finance: Last year, due to bad debts from dealings with various clients in the banking sector, most loans could not be recovered. Pledged goods also couldn't be auctioned off due to low prices. Mortgage properties yielded meager returns, with no cash available. Therefore, banks have uniformly halted lending this year, only accepting deposits and not disbursing loans. Before the new year, only a small amount was loaned out under the county government's responsibility to maintain the clearing of banknotes and provide relief to the poor. All other loans were suspended. Local money shops, since the abolition of the "Gui Yuan" system, could neither issue banknotes nor operate as northern-style banks, so they had to close down. It's estimated that banks like Tongxinggong and Jucheng have already announced their closure. The financial situation this year is expected to be even tighter. (2) Southern Goods Businesses: This sector's capital has always been known to be substantial, leading all sectors. Its history in Xuzhou is also relatively long, with businesses clustered in the southern district. Names like Zhou Shunji, Zhuang Dingji, Yang Jianji, and Jiang Houji have long been known for their reliability, with Zhuang Houji's brand being the oldest, nearing a century. However, last year, it suffered total losses, and Jiang Houji has already announced its closure. Zhuang Dingji plans to use its property to offset debts but hasn't received creditor approval, so it's barely maintaining operations. This year, it's expected to be difficult to turn things around. (3) Silk, Satin, and Cloth Businesses: The sales market for silk fabrics and cotton yarn is mainly in rural areas. In recent years, the rural economy has collapsed, and purchasing power has disappeared, severely impacting business. Furthermore, foreign cloth and yarn have predominantly been Japanese goods. The blockade of sources has also made business difficult. Hengfeng Yarn Shop, Juyuan Silk Store, and others have closed down, totaling fifteen or sixteen establishments. There's absolutely no hope for revival this year. The vitality of the countryside cannot be restored in a short time, nor can the sales of yarn and cloth be smoothed in a short time either. (4) General Merchandise and Porcelain Businesses: This sector isn't confined to any particular type of product, which is better than other sectors with fixed scopes. However, there have been no profits to be made in recent years either. Newly opened stores like Fu Da Xiang and Zhi Da have all closed down. Only older brands like Tian Cheng, Tian Fu, Hua Feng Tai, and Yang Taiji can still maintain operations, but they are also tightening their belts significantly. (5) Book Businesses: Since the summer of last year, the competition between Shanghai Bookstore and Puyu Bookstore as distributors of Commercial Press books has led to massive price reductions. The World, China, Datong, and other bookstores were swept into the vortex, competing to sell, resulting in losses for all stores. (6) Pharmaceutical Businesses: The sales market for Western pharmaceuticals is also unreliable. Usually, venereal disease drugs sell well, but now, with societal decline and economic tightening, the number of people with these ailments has also decreased. Examining the total revenue of each pharmacy will reveal this. (7) Other Businesses: Although restaurants, tea houses, soy sauce, wine, tobacco, oil, and grain businesses sell daily necessities, their business has also decreased significantly due to the economic downturn, and their profits are meager. Comparatively, soy sauce, wine, and oil businesses fare slightly better because the value of food grains is very low, and the products they produce still have slightly better profits. However, due to the impact of these closures and declines, each store has reduced staff or completely shut down, resulting in the unemployment of three to four thousand people. This is truly a major danger to society, and each store employee's family is unknown, with how many people are dependent on their livelihood. This is an even greater social problem. (February 18th)

Wuhu's Rice and Finance Industries

丨Extreme Decline in the Past Year丨

Yanhu dispatch: According to a survey after the conclusion of the Wuhu rice market, the amount exported to Guangzhou, Chaozhou, Yantai, and Ningbo last year was about two million piculs. In the past, the annual figure was consistently five to six million piculs. The fact that it has declined so much now is really due to the dumping of foreign rice. After the conclusion, the rice industry opened for business on the 16th. The price per bag increased by about four or five cents. Nanling high-grade rice was priced at four taels and four maces and one fen to two maces and four fen; Jiangbei high-grade rice was priced at four taels and one mace to four taels; medium-grade rice was priced at three taels, nine maces and two fen to eight maces and four fen; Nanling indica brown rice was priced at three taels, nine maces and two fen to eight maces and eight fen. Two years ago, there were still more than thirty money shops in Wuhu. Last year, there were only eleven, and only three or four of them actually did business with cargo stores. The rest were just open to collect debts, as they have already been monopolized by the banking sector. Yesterday, Tonghe Money Shop suddenly ran aground. This shop was one of the most well-established and historically significant money businesses in the area, with substantial capital. It went bankrupt due to excessive accounts receivable causing cash flow problems. After the abolition of the tael and the adoption of the yuan, the entire money industry is undergoing natural elimination and is about to disappear from the market. (18th)

Verdict in Hankou Racecourse Robbery Case

丨Four Robbers, Wang, Xue, Ding, and Tian, All Sentenced to Death丨

丨Three People, Including Yang Huaizhi, Acquitted丨

Hankou dispatch: The Hankou International Racecourse robbery case, which was cracked through a design by the garrison headquarters, resulted in the arrest of four robbers, Wang Xianzhang, Xue Yaoting, Ding Yuzhai, and Tian Huating. After interrogation by the military court, they were found guilty and sentenced according to the law. The execution will take place soon. The main points of the verdict are as follows: Wang Xianzhang hid in the concession, using it as a shield. He specialized in selling morphine, and his crime is unforgivable. Putting aside the case itself, he gathered bandits in his residence beforehand to plan the robbery and divided the loot in his residence afterward. It can be seen that Wang's residence was the main camp for the accomplices in this case, and Wang himself was the mastermind and principal offender in this case. Xue Yaoting was responsible for the firearms and had planned for a long time. He confessed to the stolen money, and the amount was significant. He is an important principal offender, on par with Wang. Both should be sentenced to death in accordance with Article 43 of the Criminal Law and Article 1, Section 9 of the Provisional Regulations for Punishing Bandits. Ding and Tian, both armed with firearms, carried out the robbery and subsequently divided the loot. Although the shooting and killing of the bandit Qi Chang can be seen as divine justice, it also shows the viciousness of these individuals. They should also be sentenced to death in accordance with the law for their involvement in robbery and dividing the loot. Yang Huaizhi has no fixed occupation and has long been a local rogue in Hankou. He was arrested due to mistaken identity and nearly suffered an injustice due to a car driver's false testimony. However, thanks to his help in capturing several principal offenders, all of whom said Yang was not involved, he had no criminal act. Tian Zijing and Tian Zihou, although from the same village and clan as the bandit Tian, did not participate and even pointed out the bandit Tian, showing they had no ulterior motives. Both were acquitted. Guo Wenqi received money sent by the bandit Ding, knowing its source, and showed no regard for the law. He should be sentenced to imprisonment for two years and six months. Zhang Yaonan's possession of two pistols for safekeeping and a damaged gun handed over to the Anlu County Office should be confiscated. Guo Wenqi possessed 270 yuan of stolen money sent by the bandit Ding, and Xue confessed to depositing 340 yuan of stolen money from the Central China Bank and 1,200 yuan of stolen money from the Zhejiang Industrial Bank, which were confirmed to be items stolen from the racecourse. All should be returned in full. (February 18th)

Songjiang

Defense Corps Captures Bandits and Sends Them to the County

Yangqiao Temple in Xiaokunshan Township, the 9th district of the county, has no monks or Taoists residing there. It is only inhabited by Zhuang Mo, a pious village woman who manages the incense. It was previously robbed and burglarized, but the case has not been solved. Unexpectedly, at 10 PM on the 13th, five bandits armed with guns suddenly came again, broke into the temple, tied up Mo Zhuang, and ransacked the place before leaving. The next morning, the incident was reported to the sub-station for investigation. Inspector Liu Binchen, along with the district chief of the defense corps, Xia Shutian, went to investigate. Yu Bolu, a training officer at the district headquarters, was also patrolling the Yangqiao riverside area when he saw a houseboat on the river that looked suspicious. The bandits, seeing the training officer, were afraid they were being pursued and fired shots in resistance. After about several minutes, as it was nighttime, the villagers sounded gongs to surround and capture them. Two of the bandits went ashore and fled, but Yu, the training officer, captured two of them, identified as Yao Hecheng and Shi Aqi. They denied the allegations, but the plaintiff, Zhuang Mo, identified Yao Hecheng as one of the robbers. After recording the confession, along with a bandit boat, a report was prepared and sent to the county government for verification and handling.

Taicang

Four Businesses Announce Liquidation

Due to continuous years of disasters and poor harvests in this county, all industries are declining. Following the liquidation of Jitai Pawnshop in the city on New Year's Eve, four more businesses, Wanchengxiang Southern Goods Store, Tongchangxiang Southern Goods Store, Deyuantai Silk and Cloth Store, and Zhengtai Silk and Cloth Store, officially announced liquidation on the 18th.

Suzhou

Several Rice Businesses Close

Various industries in Suzhou have successively opened for business since the 19th. In the rice industry, after the year-end settlement, except for Yuanfengyi, Jiutaiyi, Daji, and several other stores that closed, most others were able to maintain operations. A few, such as Zhenlonghong and Yitai, had surpluses. The county has a total of over 300,000 piculs of rice in stock, and rice stores also have over 100,000 piculs in stock. However, it is a matter of concern that the rural areas in the four townships have depleted their reserves. Also, because urban women are cutting their hair and rural areas are bankrupt, the number of customers for jewelry has decreased. Tongfengyong Gold Shop in West Central Market has announced its closure.

Villagers Robbed in Yinshan Township

Xu Shisheng's house in Beibang Village, Yinshan, was suddenly robbed by more than ten bandits in the middle of the night the other day. Xu resisted the bandits, and they injured his head and back. It is estimated that over a hundred yuan worth of clothing, jewelry, and cash were stolen. Then the bandits went to Xu Shaopeng's house nearby and robbed him before escaping north.

Ban on Flower Drum Opera

The New Central Theater in North Bureau was performing a flower drum opera with lewd content, with men and women mixed together, singing obscene songs, which was harmful to public morals. Yesterday, the Public Security Bureau ordered a ban, and violators will be arrested.

Wuxi

Ye Chucang Visits Wuxi for Sightseeing

Central Committee member Ye Chucang arrived in Wuxi by train from Beijing the afternoon before yesterday. Accompanied by County Magistrate Yan, he visited famous scenic spots such as Yuantouzhu, Xiaojishan, and Meiyuan. He stayed at the Meiyuan Taihu Hotel that night and left Wuxi by train to return to Beijing yesterday morning.

Car Accident Caused by Damaged Vehicle

Yesterday (19th) at 11 AM, a car with license number 269, carrying eight passengers from the city to Jiangyin, was driving through Yangsibatou in the 5th district of this county. A screw suddenly fell off the car, causing it to drive into a field and injure passenger Lu Meisheng's left foot. Other passengers only suffered minor injuries. The driver immediately called for another car to take the injured person to Jiangyin Hospital for treatment.

Bengbu Grain Merchants Oppose Commission Increase

Wuxi Rice, Bean, and Miscellaneous Grain Association saw a sharp fall in prices and poor business last year, while expenses were increasing daily. The original 99% exchange rate was insufficient to cover costs. It was previously resolved to increase the exchange rate to 98.4%, but the 8th district association failed to agree, and the change could not be implemented. After repeated consultations and a joint effort with the Wujin association, it was unanimously decided that from February 18th, all rice, paddy, wheat, yellow mung beans, and other miscellaneous grains would be converted to a 98.4% exchange rate. A public announcement was made in the newspaper. However, the Bengbu Rice Merchants Association, the Bengbu Transportation Association, and the Jiangsu Bengbu Grain Merchants Association stated that during this time of rural economic collapse, grain prices were falling, and farmers and merchants were struggling. Yellow beans are oilseeds and cannot be compared to grains. In recent years, bean prices have fallen more sharply than in the past, while transportation costs have increased instead of decreasing. Selling prices cannot improve, and various losses have become unsustainable. Yesterday, they submitted separate petitions to the Wuxi and Changzhou county governments, requesting a ban. At the same time, they appointed Sun Yuanfu, Li Peisheng, and Qian Xiaosheng as representatives to directly negotiate with the rice, bean, and miscellaneous grain associations in Wuxi and Changzhou, and telegraphed the county government and chamber of commerce, requesting assistance in addressing the difficulties.

Yangzhou

Scant Profits for the Finance Industry

The Yangzhou finance industry plummeted last year. Few businesses made a profit this year. Today (18th), only a dozen or so businesses, including Dachang (a reorganized Shengyuan), reopened as usual. In addition, Yuanchang is still under consideration by its shareholders. Liu Jingyi, who previously ran Kaibaoxing Fuyi, has recovered the store and property and plans to resume business in March. Hongda Mostly Stores Hengchang Zengfu on Jiaochang Street have all confirmed their closure.

Nantong

Provincial Order to Recover Confiscated Reclaimed Land

The provincial government, after investigation by provincial and ministry committees, has determined that Xu Daochun of Nantong has illegally occupied 1,500 mu of Liuhaisha reclaimed land. All of it has been confiscated and sold, and the money will be deposited into the national treasury. However, Xu resisted and was detained in the county government for over a year. Now, the provincial government has ordered County Magistrate Cheng to execute the order. Xu Daochun has complied with the order to hand over the land and will be released immediately.

Jiashan

County Government Orders Payment of Overdue Rent

Since taking office, the new County Magistrate of this county, Yang Zhanchun, has paid special attention to the land tax. Recognizing that the tax comes from rent, he wants to actively rectify the land tax by first rectifying land rent. He has specifically ordered all detained tenant farmers who are being held for owing rent this year to provide reliable shopkeepers as guarantors for their release, but they must pay the full amount within half a month, otherwise they will be dealt with according to the law.

Kidnapping Bandits Arrested

A few days ago, the farmer Meng Youfa's house in Zhuxiaowan, this county, was broken into by more than ten bandits, who ransacked the place, losing a lot of cash and clothing. Before leaving, they kidnapped Meng's son, Baisheng. The Meng family prepared money, contacted them, and paid a ransom for his release. Yesterday, the 7th Water Police Team sent police to track down and arrest three of the kidnappers, Meng Agen, Qi Zhongguang, and others, and brought them to the county. County Magistrate Yang personally interrogated them and has now transferred them to the court for interrogation.

Xiaoshan

Qianjiang Ferry Passenger Statistics

Due to the opening of the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Road, passengers on the Qianjiang ferry in Xiaoshan mostly took the ferry, and the number of business cars decreased in 1932, so the number of ferry passengers suddenly increased. The total number of ferry passengers for the whole year was 5,819,316, with a daily average of 15,943, an increase of one-third over the previous year.

Local News

Mourning for the Death of the Belgian King

Mayor Wu and others visited the Belgian Consulate General yesterday to express condolences

All agencies lowered flags to half-mast for three days starting yesterday

After the sad news of the death of King Albert I of Belgium spread, all countries around the world mourned in unison. Our country has also sent a telegram to the Belgian Queen to express condolences. At the same time, all Chinese and foreign agencies in the city lowered their flags to half-mast for three days starting yesterday to show their mourning. The Belgian Consul General in China, Delfaux, also hosted guests at the consulate yesterday to express their condolences. Details are as follows:

Our Country Expresses Condolences Yesterday, according to diplomatic sources, after the death of the Belgian King, in addition to our minister to Belgium, Zhang Naiyan, representing our country to express condolences to the Belgian government, Chairman Lin of the National Government and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs have also sent telegrams to the Belgian Queen to express condolences.

Belgian Consulate Reception Yesterday morning and afternoon, dignitaries from various Chinese and foreign agencies in this city visited the Belgian Consulate on Route Lafayette in the French Concession to express their condolences. Consul General Delfaux hosted the reception. Those who went to express their condolences yesterday included Shanghai Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Director Yu Ming of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs' Shanghai Office, Cuban Minister Piedra, Japanese Minister Arima Akira, Swiss Chargé d'Affaires Anfuso, Swedish Chargé d'Affaires Lindquist, US Consul General Cunningham, Dutch Consul General Groneman, Italian Consul General Nailon, French Consul General Meyrier, German Consul General Behrend, Portuguese Consul General Silva, Japanese Consul General Ishisha, Norwegian Consul General Hansen, Secretary General of the Consular Corps Lange, Danish Consul General Lunds, Jianghai Customs representative Brandt, and Vice Director of the Catholic Church Xiang Kean, among others.

Half-Mast for Three Days In addition to personally visiting the Belgian Consulate to express condolences, leaders of Chinese and foreign agencies in this city, including the Municipal Government, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs Office, and the consulates of Britain, the United States, France, Italy, Japan, Germany, Denmark, the Netherlands, and Portugal, all lowered their flags to half-mast to show their mourning. According to sources from the Consular Corps, the consulates of all countries will lower their flags to half-mast for three days, starting yesterday and resuming their original flag positions on the 22nd of this month. In addition, the Catholic Church in the French Concession also held prayers for the Belgian King yesterday. The Ta Mei Evening News reported that this morning (19th), the British naval authorities stationed in Shanghai received orders to fly all the ships under their command at half-mast to express their condolences for the death of King Albert of Belgium. The period is subject to further orders. It is expected that warships from other countries will receive similar orders sooner or later, as all countries in the world are now mourning the late King of Belgium.

Belgian Envoy's Memorial The Continental Daily reported that Fang Fei, the acting Belgian Consul General in Shanghai, intends to postpone the memorial service for King Albert of Belgium until the Belgian Minister to China, Ji Youmu, arrives in Shanghai from Beijing within a few days. It is said that they are currently discussing holding a memorial service at St. Joseph's Catholic Church.

Xie Shoukang's Telegram Former Minister to Belgium Dr. Xie Shoukang had a very close relationship with the royal family during his tenure. After hearing the news, he personally went to the Belgian Embassy to express condolences and sent a telegram to the Belgian Queen. The text is as follows: "The late King fostered friendly relations between China and Belgium, which I deeply admire. I am overwhelmed with sorrow at this unexpected event. I beg you to accept my condolences and maintain the country."

Zhang Xueliang Went to Beijing Yesterday

Will Stay in Beijing for About a Week

Will Go Directly to Hankou to Assume New Position

The newly appointed Deputy Commander of the Bandit Suppression in the three provinces of Henan, Anhui, and Hubei, Zhang Xueliang, accompanied by his secretary Wu Jiaxiang, Shen Zutong, Adjutant General Tang Guozhen, Guard Captain Tan Hai, advisor Donner, and others, took the night train to Beijing last night. They boarded the train from Zhenru Station. According to Zhang's staff, Zhang plans to stay in Beijing for about a week, meeting with various central authorities, and then go directly to Hankou to take up his new post. As for the timing of his trip north to visit his family, it will be decided after he takes office.

Li Du Returns to Shanghai Today

The decision to go to Xinjiang is made by the Central Government

Three Ways to Settle the Families of Soldiers

General Li Du, the former commander of the Jilin Self-Defense Army, went to Tianjin to meet with General Ma Zhanshan. Having completed his business, he left Tianjin and returned to Shanghai. The National News Agency reporter met Mr. Wang Ziyao, the former chief of staff of the army, at his residence on Jing'an Temple Road yesterday. According to the conversation, General Li will arrive in Shanghai this afternoon. The recorded details of the conversation are as follows:

Welcoming Li to Xinjiang

After the reporter met Mr. Wang, he first inquired about Li's trip to Xinjiang to gather his old troops. Wang replied that a month ago, Li, seeing that his troops in Xinjiang had no one in charge, had the intention to go there. Also, the new province sent a telegram expressing welcome, saying that the situation surrounding provincial governor Sheng Shicai and Ma Zhongying was complicated, that the troops and officers stationed in the border area numbered ten thousand, and that they hoped he would come to Xinjiang to gather them and await review by the Central Government. Therefore, General Li had the intention to go to Xinjiang, but whether he would enter Xinjiang must be decided by the Central Government. If the Central Government orders him to go, he will set off immediately. General Li received a telegram the day before yesterday, saying that he was allowed to arrive in Shanghai on the 20th. As for the troops remaining in Xinjiang, there are more than 8,600, of which more than 2,100 are the old troops of General Su Bingwen, who are commanded by the Jilin Office. The rest are from the Jilin Self-Defense Army, led by Commander Zheng Runcheng. Currently, all supplies and clothing are provided by Chairman Sheng, but each soldier only receives one yuan per month in salary, so their lives are extremely difficult. They all hope that the Central Government can quickly reorganize them formally.

Families Stranded in Tianjin and Shanghai

Afterward, Mr. Wang told the reporter that a total of 340 families of Jilin officers and soldiers who fled from the Northeast to Russia are currently in Shanghai, nearly 200 in Tianjin, and over 40 in Beiping. Most of these families have men still in Xinjiang, so the problem of livelihood is extremely difficult to solve. Of these 340 people, one-third are families of General Su's troops. Wang's (Wang referring to himself) stay in Shanghai is also due to being held up by handling this matter. Now, three methods of settlement have been sought and submitted to the Central Government, because the Central Government cannot bear to see the families of meritorious soldiers in the Northeast continue to be displaced. The methods are divided into three steps: (1) Settle the officers, who can earn money themselves, so their families will not worry about poverty. (2) Send the families to Xinjiang, because most of the female relatives have husbands who are still stationed far away. (3) Find ways to support themselves. Among these three methods, the third, supporting themselves, is the most difficult, because Jilin people face great difficulties in finding work in East China due to language barriers. Furthermore, it is even more difficult to find a way out due to unfamiliarity with the area. Therefore, this matter is currently being handled by me, and I believe that a better solution will be found in the shortest possible time.

Eurasia Company Tests Ping-Shan Line

Li Jingcong Flew from Ping to Bing Yesterday

Eurasia Aviation is planning to open the Ping-Shan and Yue-Shan air routes. General Manager Li Jingcong went to Beiping in person. Yesterday afternoon, he took off from Ping on a test flight, passing through Taiyuan and arriving in Xi'an. Then, he flew back to Shanghai from Shan via Hankou. After staying in Shanghai for a day or two, he will go to Guangdong to inspect the airport. For the time being, the Northwest trunk line cannot reach Xinjiang. Details are as follows:

Ping-Shan Test Flight To open the Ping-Shan air route, Eurasia Aviation is conducting a preliminary test flight. General Manager Li Jingcong arrived in Beiping a few days ago. The second test flight plane flew to Beiping last Saturday. It was originally scheduled to take off from Ping today (Tuesday), but Li was eager to prepare for the opening of the Ping-Shan and Yue-Shan routes, so he advanced the takeoff to yesterday. He left Ping at around 1 PM, arrived in Taiyuan that day, and stayed to discuss airport and station establishment matters. Then he left Bing and flew to Xi'an. After arriving in Xi'an, he took the original plane along the planned Yue-Shan air route via Xiangyang and arrived in Hankou, and then returned to Shanghai east.

Guangzhou Airport The Yue-Shan line was originally scheduled to open on the 6th of this month, but the Guangdong Provincial Government said that it was inconvenient for civil aviation to borrow the Guangzhou Shougouling military airfield. Guangzhou originally planned to add a civil airport, and the site has been designated. The Guangzhou Municipal Government was ordered to expedite construction so that it could be completed as soon as possible and used for the Yue-Shan air route aircraft to land. As a result, it was temporarily unable to open. Later, there was a suggestion that the racetrack could be temporarily borrowed. The company believes that whether the racetrack is suitable and when the civil airport can be completed both require on-site inspection. Therefore, General Manager Li Jingzong, after returning to Shanghai from Hankou, will spend a day or two and then go to Guangdong with the engineers to open the Yue-Shan line as soon as possible.

Resuming Flights to Xinjiang Previous reports said that Nanjing Electric reported that Sheng Shicai had telegraphed the Eurasia Company requesting to resume flights to Dihua before the 28th of this month. Yesterday, a newspaper also reported that the company was already preparing for this. According to Secretary Cha Zhen of the company, speaking to the New Voice News reporter, the company has been planning to resume flights to Xinjiang all the time. However, in fact, it has been unable to proceed due to the ongoing war. The Hami station between Dihua and Gansu is still under the control of Ma Zhongying. With the war not yet over, it is difficult to achieve for the time being. As for Sheng Shicai's telegram request, the company has not yet received it.

Zheng Baozhao Transferred to Deputy Director of Beining Railway

Xiao Weiguo Appointed Director of Car Affairs of the Two Railways

Municipal Defense Committee Officially Established Yesterday

All Members Swore an Oath of Office at the Municipal Government

Yang Hu and Two Others Were Elected as Standing Committee Members

The Municipal Defense Corps has a glorious history of defending the area and assisting military police in maintaining public order for decades. However, due to the influence of the situation over the years, it has not been able to actively proceed in strengthening its organization and strengthening its forces. Mayor Wu, recognizing this, drafted the Shanghai Municipal Defense Committee Organizational Rules last year, which he consulted with the Municipal Provisional Council and passed. He also hired Yu Qiaqing, Wang Xiaolai, Du Yuesheng, Yao Mulian, Wang Binyan, Luo Weixiong, Wang Yansong, Yang Hu, Wen Hongen, Wu Xingya, and others as members. At 10:10 AM yesterday

Ten, at the expanded memorial week in the new city government auditorium in the city center, the establishment ceremony of the Shanghai Municipal Defense Committee was held.

Inauguration of Committee Members

Yesterday's attendees included Chairman Wu Tiecheng, Committee Members Yao Mulian, Wang Xiaolai, Yu Qiaqing, Wang Binyan, Yang Hu, Wu Xingya, Wen Hongen, Du Yuesheng, and over forty others, including the heads and deputies of various district corps from the entire city. Staff members Wang Yansong and Luo Weixiong were absent due to matters requiring them to leave Shanghai. Mayor Wu, as chairman, presided over the ceremony, and the committee members took their oaths of office. The oath read: "I solemnly swear that I will respectfully adhere to the will of the late Premier Sun Yat-sen, obey the principles of the party, follow the directives of the central government and higher authorities, respect the public opinion of the local people, and be loyal and diligent in my duties. If I violate this oath, I am willing to accept the most severe punishment. This is my oath."

Mayor's Address

After the swearing-in ceremony, Chairman and Mayor Wu delivered a speech, saying, "Fellow comrades, today marks the establishment of the Shanghai Municipal Defense Committee, and the members have been sworn into office. In his entire body of teachings, the late Premier Sun Yat-sen very specifically instructed us that the process of nation-building should be based on local self-government as the fundamental task, and that local self-defense is one of the prerequisites for local self-government. Therefore, the Outline of National Reconstruction clearly states that local autonomy can only be discussed once local defense and security are properly managed. The defense corps is a force for local self-defense and an organization for local security. Although our Shanghai Municipal Defense Corps has a long and glorious history, due to various factors such as time, financial resources, and local incidents, its organization and training have not met the expectations of the citizens of Shanghai. The Shanghai Municipal Government, based on the Provisional Regulations for Local Defense Organizations promulgated by the central government, has drafted the organizational rules for the Shanghai Municipal Defense Committee, which have been approved by the Shanghai Municipal Provisional Council. This committee is hereby established today, and all members are sworn into office. From now on, all members should work together with the government to shoulder the heavy responsibility of local self-defense, and gradually improve and strengthen the organization and capabilities of the local defense corps, in order to promote the completion of local autonomy. How to reorganize and improve the defense corps in the future is not only the responsibility of all committee members, but also requires soliciting the opinions of all parties in the local community to ensure that we fulfill our mission. This is what the Shanghai Municipal Defense Committee hopes for from all sectors of the city upon its establishment today."

Inauguration of the Municipal Defense Corps Committee (Photo by Wang Kai)

Only when we manage local defence and security properly, can we discuss the completion of local autonomy

Election of Standing Committee Members

After Mayor Wu's address, the first committee meeting was held in the municipal government's conference room. Wu Tiecheng, Yang Hu, Wen Hongen, Wu Xingya, Yao Mulian, Wang Binyan, Wang Xiaolai, and Du Yuesheng were present, totaling eight people. Mayor Wu presided over the meeting, and Yao Mulian, Wang Binyan, and Yang Hu were unanimously elected as standing committee members. It was decided that the first standing committee meeting would be held on the 23rd. Finally, a group photo was taken in front of the municipal government before adjourning.

List of Corps

The list of corps heads and deputies of the Shanghai Municipal Defense Committee is as follows: Jiangwan District Corps: Wu Yaying; Pengpu District Corps: Hou Qizhang; Zhenru District Corps: Wang Shouyu; Yangjing District Corps: Xu Baoming, Shen Wenbin; Caojing District Corps: Yang Xinzheng; Yinhang District Corps: Zhou Dai, Zhu Jiazhen; Fahua District Corps: Li Chao, Xu Lianke; Lixing District Corps: Zhao Yuanshou; Hunan District Corps: Yao Mulian; Tangqiao District Corps: Wang Hui; Zhabei District Corps: Wang Dong, Gu Zhuxuan; Yangsi District Corps: Chen Tianxi; Wusong District Corps: Tang Chengzong.

Yang Shuzhuang's Funeral Held Yesterday

Chen Shaokuan, Wu Tiecheng, and others personally helped with the coffin.

The coffin was transported by the Tongji warship to Fujian.

Yang Shuzhuang, a member of the Central Executive Committee of the Nationalist Government and a naval veteran, passed away at his Shanghai residence on the 10th of last month. His coffin was temporarily placed in the International Funeral Parlor on Jiaozhou Road. After the Nationalist Government issued an order for a public funeral, the funeral was held yesterday afternoon, and the coffin was transported back to his ancestral home in Fujian by the Tongji warship. Yesterday's funeral was exceptionally grand, with the Minister of the Navy, Chen Shaokuan, leading all officers and men along the way, totaling no less than twenty thousand people. At 5:00 PM, the coffin arrived at the Tongji warship below Gaochang Temple. At 7:00 PM, a banquet was held at the Yizhixiang Western Restaurant on Fourth Avenue to entertain guests from all walks of life who assisted with the funeral.

Details of the Procession: Yang Shuzhuang's coffin departed from the International Funeral Parlor on Jiaozhou Road at 1:00 PM yesterday afternoon. In front of the Flour Exchange on Minguo Road, the Siming Guild Hall and the Xiaoximen Youth Propaganda Corps were hosted by representatives from the funeral affairs office, who provided tea and refreshments. Those from all walks of life who assisted with and saw off the funeral procession included Chief of Staff Zhu Peide, Shanghai Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Minister of the Navy Chen Shaokuan, Commander of the Training Fleet Wang Shouting, Commander of the Xiamen Naval Base Lin Guogeng, Deputy Director of the Jiangnan Shipyard Chen Zaofan, Director of the Hydrographic Office Liu Defu, Director of the Coastal Patrol Wu Zhennan, Director of the Aircraft Manufacturing Office Zeng Yijing, Director of the Ordnance Office Zheng Zizhi, the captains and officers of the warships stationed in Shanghai, including Yixian, Tongji, Hairong, Zhongshan, and Yongji, the commander of the Marine Corps Guard Battalion Ye Baoqi, the chairman of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Wang Xiaolai, the Director of the Public Security Bureau Wen Hongen, Central Committee member Fang Shengtao, and dignitaries and businessmen such as Du Yuesheng, Wang Yiting, Yu Qiaqing, and the counselor of the Polish embassy.

Grand Ceremony: The funeral procession was very grand and solemn. The Public Security Bureau dispatched a police brigade, a mobile patrol team, and police officers from the first and second districts, armed to maintain order along the route and maintain strict security. The French Concession police also sent Chinese and foreign detectives to guard the Minguo Road area. The procession began at 1:00 PM, and preparation was made for the departure from Laobeimen to Xinkai Road, a distance of about one mile. The procession began at 2:00 PM. Many citizens lined the streets to watch, causing traffic congestion. The trams on Fahua Third Road were temporarily suspended. The route departed from Xinkaihe, passed through Zhonghua Road, turned onto Shangwen Road, entered Daxing Street, Chezhan Hou Road, turned onto Hu Min Nan Ku Road, entered Chezhan Road Yingpan Road, and finally reached Gaochang Temple Wharf. Guests assisting with the funeral procession dispersed from the Siming Guild Hall on Minguo Road to the entrance of the Xiaoximen Youth Propaganda Corps.

Arrangement of the Order: The procession was led by the police brigade and mobile patrol team of the Public Security Bureau, with the flags of the party and nation, and the personal standard of Yang Shuzhuang, a member of the Central Executive Committee of the Nationalist Government and Admiral of the Navy, carried by soldiers of the Hairong warship riding white horses. Following them was the military band of the Municipal Public Security Bureau and a company of armed police officers, a car carrying a commendation order from the Nationalist Government decorated with plain colors, the military band of the Garrison Headquarters, a squad of armed soldiers from the Shanghai Security Team, a car carrying a public funeral order from the Nationalist Government decorated with plain colors, guests who assisted with the funeral procession, a car carrying a portrait of the deceased, a shock flag team, the naval band, sailors and marines from warships such as Tongji, Hairong, Yixian, Zhongshan, Yongji, and Yongjian, a company of soldiers from the Marine Corps Guard Battalion, naval students, those in military uniforms and plain clothing, and finally the filial sons. The coffin was surrounded by sailors from the Hairong warship, providing tight security. At the end were sailors from the Hairong and Tongji warships, followed by cars for female relatives, all of which were green cars from the Xiang Sheng Company.

Roadside Sacrifices Along the Way: There were more than thirty places in total. The roadside sacrifice for all officers and soldiers of the Navy was set up at the Siming Guild Hall on Minguo Road, and Minister Chen Shaokuan personally presided over the sacrifice. The roadside sacrifice for Central Committee member Fang Shengtao was set up at Zhuangyuanlou in Xinbeimen. The roadside sacrifice for the Second Fleet Command was set up at the intersection of Wenmiao Road. The roadside sacrifice for the Fire Brigade First Fleet Command was set up at the Xiaoximen tram station. The roadside sacrifice for the Training Fleet Command was set up at Gaochang Temple. The roadside sacrifice for the Mawei Training Camp and the Guard Battalion was set up at the entrance of Xiaobeimen. The roadside sacrifice for the Jiangnan Shipyard was set up at the entrance of the Radio Station on Minguo Road.

Coffin Lowered onto the Ship: Yang's eldest son, Zhihong, was unable to return home for the funeral due to studying in England. At yesterday's funeral, Yang's two daughters, Lingshu and Xinshu, escorted the coffin. At 5:30 PM, they arrived at Gaochang Temple and lowered it onto the Tongji warship. The ship was docked at the shipyard wharf and had already been fired up, ready to depart. Today it will load coal, and on the 22nd, it will set sail. The Yang family will escort the coffin back to their ancestral home in Fuzhou, Fujian, and will arrive there on the evening of the 23rd. After arriving in Fujian, the Fujian Provincial Government will select a date for the public funeral.

China National Aviation Corporation Increases Flights on Two Routes

The China National Aviation Corporation has been actively expanding its business on its existing routes. Details are recorded below:

Shanghai-Guangdong Section

The Shanghai-Guangdong route has always been very crowded. Only the No. 16 Stinson aircraft was damaged near Zhabu, so only the No. 17 Stinson aircraft flew back and forth on the route, which was quite overwhelming. Now, a new twin-engine aircraft newly purchased from the United States has arrived in Shanghai, and it will be fully assembled soon. Once the test flight is satisfactory, it will be added to the Shanghai-Guangdong route. The company has scheduled flights from Shanghai to Guangdong every Tuesday and Friday, and from Guangdong to Shanghai every Wednesday and Saturday. The plan to fly the new aircraft to Guangdong on the 23rd of this month has been postponed to early March because the new aircraft is not yet fully assembled, so the plan to fly twice a week will be implemented.

Hankou-Chongqing Route

The number of passengers and detailed items on the section from Hankou to Chongqing on the company's Shanghai-Chengdu route are extremely crowded. The company has decided to increase the number of flights on this section by one per week, with flights from Hankou to Chongqing every Monday, Wednesday, and Friday, and flights from Chongqing to Hankou every Tuesday, Thursday, and Saturday. As for the implementation date, it is also expected to be in early March.

Hong Kong Station

The company's planned China-Philippines route, which has been test-flown once, uses Hong Kong and Manila as important transit stations. The negotiations for setting up a station in Hong Kong have been discussed many times. However, the rumor that the company's senior executive, Mr. Bixby, went to Hankou to negotiate is not true. Mr. Bixby, an American director of the company, returned to the United States for personal reasons two months ago and has not yet come to China.

Japanese Ambassador Arima to Go to Beijing Tonight

The Japanese Ambassador to China, Akira Ariyoshi, will leave Shanghai for Beijing on the 11:00 PM Shanghai-Beijing express train tonight, accompanied by Counselor Horiuchi and Chinese Secretary Arino, due to negotiations on issues in North China. According to Mr. Arino, Ariyoshi's trip to Beijing has no specific task, but is merely a routine visit to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. After arriving in Beijing, he will stay for about a day and then return to Shanghai. As for his return to Japan, he has this intention, but the date has not yet been determined. It is expected to be in March or April. Arino did not explicitly state the specific task of the ambassador's trip, and denied the various pending issues in North China as reported in the newspapers.

International Trade Bureau Announces Discovery of Gold Dust in Rivers of Jixi County

Farmers Pan for Gold to Make a Living

According to a message released yesterday by the International Trade Bureau, in addition to the abundant timber production in the mountains of various counties in Anhui Province, the coal reserves are also extremely rich. However, the metallic mineral content in the sandy and gravelly mountains and various rivers is also not insignificant, but due to inconvenient transportation, few people pay attention to mining, resulting in the good resources being buried underground for a long time. Recently, a large amount of gold dust ore was discovered in the 15th District of Jixi County, located at the foot of Li Da Cen under Wanduan Jinguang Cen. Gold dust is found in the river about thirty miles from Cen Jiao to Ge Xi. In recent years, due to the bankruptcy of the rural economy, no less than four or five hundred farmers in the vicinity have been panning for gold to make a living. The total value of gold obtained by the farmers is also four or five thousand yuan. Zhang Jiesheng, the head of the county's construction department, recently went to the area to investigate and drafted a report to the authorities to find ways to mine it. In the future, when the Wuhu-Tunxi highway is completed and transportation is convenient, if we can actively raise funds for mining and refining, it will be a great source of profit.

Representatives of the Federation of Trade Unions Went to Beijing Last Night to Petition the Central Government

Trade Unions Jointly Petition for Amendment of the Trade Union Law

In order to request the central government to decide on the representatives to the upcoming International Labour Conference and to demand the amendment of the Trade Union Law, the Shanghai Federation of Trade Unions, after deliberation at its standing committee meeting, appointed Zhou Xuexiang, Li Mengnan, Long Peiyun, and Shao Xubai as committee members to go to Beijing to petition. The representatives have already taken the petition and boarded the night express train to Beijing last night. Many trade union representatives went to the station to see them off. The details are as follows:

Went to Beijing Last Night

The federation believes that the upcoming International Labour Conference is about to open, but the labor representatives have not yet been determined. Previously, it had telegraphed the central government, suggesting that one to three people be elected by the labor circles in various places, and then one person be selected by the central government, but this was not adopted. The federation believes that the conference is imminent, and it is deeply concerned that the central government will temporarily appoint representatives who do not conform to the public opinion of the labor circles, so it specially appointed Zhou Xuexiang, Shao Xubai, Long Peiyun, and Li Mengnan as committee members to go to Beijing to petition the Central People's Movement Committee and the Ministry of Industry. At the same time, the various trade unions in the city, regarding the organizational problems of the Municipal Federation of Trade Unions, jointly prepared a petition requesting the amendment of the Trade Union Law. The petition was also handed over to the representatives to take to Beijing. The representatives boarded the night express train to Beijing last night. Representatives of various trade unions, including Zhu Xuefan, Ye Xianggao, Fan Yifeng, Su Shaotao, Zhang Linhua, Liu Xinquan, and Zhao Zhenhui, all went to the station to welcome them and took photos at the North Station to commemorate the occasion.

Petition

To the Central Committee, regarding the matter of submitting a petition: We humbly note that the 18th International Labour Conference is about to open, and our government representatives have already been appointed. However, in previous sessions, the labor representatives were often not prepared in advance, and were either temporarily appointed by members of the Central Committee or designated by the government. As a result, the representatives attending the conference may have had no connection with the labor circles, which not only violates the provisions of the International Labour Organization's regulations, but also concerns the national image and invites ridicule from other countries. The federation, in view of this, telegraphed the Ministry a few days ago, suggesting that the labor representatives for this session should be genuine workers with full experience elected by the labor circles in various places, one to three people, and then one person should be selected by the government as the attending representative, to avoid repeating the mistakes of previous sessions. Now that the conference is imminent, the Ministry has not yet decided on a plan, so we have specially prepared a document and appointed representatives Zhou Xuexiang, Li Mengnan, Shao Xubai, Long Peiyun, etc. to go to Beijing to petition. We humbly request that the Ministry (committees) comply with public opinion and allow the representatives to be selected by the labor circles in various places for this conference. We are extremely urgent in presenting this matter. We respectfully submit this petition.

Trade Union Petitions

Various trade unions jointly petition the Central Party Department to amend the Trade Union Law, stating: Regarding the matter of requesting that the Legislative Yuan be consulted to promptly amend the Trade Union Law, it is necessary to expressly stipulate that each province and city may organize a Federation of Trade Unions, and to maintain the original organization of the Shanghai Federation of Trade Unions, so as to maintain the labor movement and benefit the revolution. After the promulgation of the Trade Union Law, only the organization of federations of various industry trade unions was permitted, and there was no provision for the organization of a Federation of Trade Unions. Labor circles and party departments in various provinces and cities deeply know that the promulgation of the regulations will cause major obstacles to the future of the labor movement, so they were panicked and repeatedly petitioned for amendments, but they were not approved. As of today, the labor movement in various places has fallen into a state of depression due to the restrictions of the law, and the facts are all there, so it is difficult to avoid mentioning them. After the September 18th Incident, the labor circles in the city are increasingly concerned about the foreign invasion, and the national fortune is declining. In order to jointly rescue the crisis, it is believed that it is impossible to succeed without aligning our steps and uniting as one. Therefore, a resolution was passed by the general assembly of representatives of various trade unions in the city, and the Shanghai Federation of Trade Unions was established. On October 2nd of last year, it was approved by the Shanghai Special City Party Department to be temporarily registered. Since the establishment of the Federation of Trade Unions, it has been three years. Because its leadership is appropriate and its command is effective, the actions of our labor circles have gradually become consistent, and their strength has also become concentrated. The depressed and chaotic labor movement in the city has been reborn and revived. Moreover, after investigation, the actions of the Federation of Trade Unions are all based on the principles of our party, and they have made their greatest efforts to cope with the national crisis. In addition, they have spared no effort in preventing communist activities, eliminating disputes in various industries to stabilize society, assisting pure worker organizations to form trade unions to increase the strength of our party, and holding labor education lectures and labor supplementary night schools to increase worker knowledge. The past achievements are well known to the labor circles throughout the city, so the affiliated associations have unanimously expressed their enthusiastic support for the Federation of Trade Unions. Unexpectedly, the Central People's Movement Committee recently ordered the name of the Federation of Trade Unions to be changed to the "National Salvation Federation of Various Industry Trade Unions" on the grounds that the Federation of Trade Unions has no legal basis, and the organization of the Federation of Trade Unions was virtually abolished. The affiliated associations were shocked and panicked to hear this. We humbly believe that the law is based on facts. The organization of the Shanghai Federation of Trade Unions is the consistent demand of the labor circles throughout the city, and the past facts prove that it is necessary for its existence. Therefore, the law should adapt to the environment and provide explicit provisions based on the needs of the facts. Furthermore, the law is based on the principle of equality. After investigation, all sectors of agriculture, commerce, and academia have general organizational provisions such as city agricultural associations, city chambers of commerce, and student federations. Only our labor circles are not allowed to have a general organization of a Federation of Trade Unions. How can this be said to be fair? The affiliated associations jointly submitted a report to the Fourth Plenary Session to request relief, but it was not submitted for discussion. We will reiterate the facts and state the reasons in detail, and jointly prepare a document to sincerely request your association to consult the Legislative Yuan to quickly amend the Trade Union Law and stipulate explicitly that each province and city may organize a Federation of Trade Unions, or promulgate a separate organizational regulation for the Shanghai Federation of Trade Unions. Before the new law is promulgated, please maintain the original organization of the Shanghai Federation of Trade Unions. The future of the labor movement is deeply reliant on it. We are extremely urgent in presenting this matter. We respectfully submit this to the Executive Committee of the Central Party Department. The following ninety-odd trade unions: Shanghai Six Districts Public Bus, Second District Rubber, Liang Industry Occupation, Five District Papermaking, Four District Papermaking, Rice Vehicle Industry, Six District Paint Making, Native Product Industry, Ship Wood Industry, Running Shoe Upper Industry, Military Uniform Industry, Postal Workers, Postal Workers, Six District Cotton Weaving, Four District Silk Reeling, Six District Silk Reeling, Leather Making Industry, Two District Knitting, Towing Industry, Three District Rubber, One District Cleaning, Five District Shipbuilding, Six District Water and Electricity, Four District Water and Wood, Six District Tea Making, Silver Building, Four District Cleaning, Four District Cotton Weaving, Four District Cigarette Rolling, Ten District Cotton Spinning, Four District Transport Towing, Four District Electrical Appliances, Sauce Industry, One District Water and Electricity, Candle Industry, One District Shipbuilding, Shanghai Ningbo Wheel Tea Room, Pharmaceutical Industry, Three District Cotton Spinning, Toothbrush Industry, Four District Rubber, Newspaper Delivery, Automobile Driver, Garment, Nine District Soap Medicine, Bristle, One District Cosmetics, One District Water and Wood, Rice Husk, Fresh Pig, Sampan Households, Ink Making, Five District Cotton Spinning, Husk Rice, Civil Ship Wood Industry, Winemaking, Duck Slaughtering, Five District Water and Wood, Five District Cigarette Rolling, Cured Meat, Aluminumware, Gas, New Year Red Electric Light, Incense Industry, One District Rubber, Chinese and Foreign Cloth Industry, Stone Printing, Shoemaking Industry.

Domestic Celebrities Regularly Commemorate Chen Qubing

According to the Central News Agency, Mr. Chen Qubing of Wujiang was a pioneer of the Party and the nation. At the end of the Qing Dynasty, he was engaged in the revolution. When Premier Sun Yat-sen organized the Tongmenghui in Tokyo, he followed him closely and participated in the revolutionary work to overthrow the Manchu Qing Dynasty. He also reorganized the Nanshe with Liu Yazi and others to advocate racial revolution through writing. At one time, domestic celebrities such as Song Yufu, Huang Xing, Yu Youren, and Dai Jitao responded and joined the organization, reaching more than a thousand people. It was the only propaganda organization of the Tongmenghui in the country. After the Xinhai Revolution, all domestic cultural groups, such as major daily newspapers and universities, mainly used members of the Nanshe as their main members. Mr. Chen had high aspirations and integrity, and did not take credit for his achievements. Except for once serving as a consultant to the Presidential Palace and a secretary to the Grand Marshal's Office, he rejected officialdom and devoted his life to teaching and writing. He successively served as a professor at Zhejiang Higher School, Zhejiang Public Law and Politics College, National Southeast University, and Shanghai Zhizhi University. Unfortunately, the sad news came that he passed away in his hometown of Tongli, Wujiang, on October 4 last year. People at home and abroad were saddened to hear the news. Shanghai Mayor Wu Tiecheng and domestic celebrities Liu Yazi, Hu Pu'an, Zhu Fengwei, Zhu Shaoping, etc., specially initiated a meeting to commemorate Mr. Chen at the Ningbo Township Association at 3:00 PM on March 4. The announcement of the memorial service stated: "We have heard of the Zhang Shao agreement of the white horse and plain carriage before his death, and the Qiao Xuan alliance of a chicken and a jug of wine after his death. The aspirations of attacking jade are sincere, and the friendship of casting gold is close. Chen Qubing came from Songling and was known throughout the world. He joined the Tongmenghui early and reorganized the Nanshe. He was like Lu Zhonglian, who did not serve Qin when surrounded by the city, and like Shen Baoxu, who was determined to restore Chu when he wept blood on the court wall. He has already illuminated the sun and the moon, and his spirit is thin. He served Premier Sun Yat-sen in Yangshi, planning strategies and advising, like Zhang Liang assisting Emperor Gaozu of Han. He relied on his strategy at the military gate, like Deng Yu following Emperor Guangwu of Han. He was always respectful, and was treated with great kindness. Ah, how prosperous he was! When Zhong Zi died, he stopped playing the strings. When Bole died, he grieved over the loss of his good horse. He hid in the forests and springs, and focused on literature and history. The national spirit has been through several years, but it has been troubled by the dragon and snake. He exhausted the treasures of the sea house, and the schools were full of sorrow and scholars wept. Is there no reason for this? We are allied in the Nanshe, and our feelings are stronger than brothers. We are saddened by the death of Chen Zhi, and we dare not be stingy with our offerings. May the pine and cypress trees provide a home for the gods of Mount Tai, and may the lychee and yellow banana trees enjoy the temple of Luo Chi for a long time. Wu Tiecheng, Liu Yazi, Hu Pu'an, Zhu Fengwei, Zhu Shaoping."

Inside the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Finance

Several Foreign Groups Participate in Rent Reduction Movement

According to a report in the Japanese-language "Shanghai Mainichi Shimbun" yesterday, the movement to reduce rents throughout Shanghai is expanding daily. The participation of various sectors in the Chinese concessions is quite enthusiastic, and all citizens support and endorse it in the hope of achieving their demands. It is estimated that more than ten foreign groups have joined in support, with Japanese, Russians, and Indians being the most numerous. The British, Americans, and other countries are also working hard to encourage the movement for the sake of promoting public welfare and stimulating the prosperity of the market. Currently, all nationalities are working together to actively promote the movement and will not give up until it is implemented. It has been found that in recent years, the price index has gradually declined, but rents have continued to increase. In terms of the standard index of 260 daily necessities and the rent index:

Since 1926, the price index has dropped by 20 percent, while rents have risen by as much as 12 percent. Moreover, the number of households has been increasing year by year, but rents have continued to rise, which is a major problem in society.
