Education News from Other Provinces

Chairman Jiang Attaches Importance to Production Education

| Instructing on Four Key Points for Implementation |

Chairman Jiang recently visited Hangzhou, and his speeches at the Provincial Government and the Aviation School focused mainly on education. It is learned that a military order was issued to Zhejiang yesterday, ordering the Provincial Government to instruct the Education and Construction Departments to prepare a production education plan for review. The original order is extracted as follows: "Political education and production are the priorities of national salvation and the foundation for national revival. When considering the powerful nations, none of them, after being devastated, did not rise up quickly and integrate production into education as an effective measure, using each other to inspire themselves and strive for strength. Only by being diligent can they succeed. When I was commanding troops in Wuhan the year before last, I deeply understood that without rectifying politics, there would be no way to eliminate the source of chaos, and without integrating education and production into one, there would be no way to achieve social stability. I issued Secret Order No. 647 to plan for the cooperation of construction and education, and Secret Order No. 539 to promulgate the General Outline of Implementation Principles for Political Education, Education Production, and Production Education. Now, it is found that the education and construction departments of various provinces and commissioners are mostly able to implement the laws earnestly, but there are also those who are still planning and handling them improperly. The key points are hereby instructed again: 1. If agricultural farms and agricultural and forestry experimental schools have not yet been prepared in the residences of the commissioners, they shall submit written plans to the competent authorities for review within ten days of receiving this document, without further delay. 2. Agricultural and forestry training classes are particularly important. If they have not been established in the residences of the commissioners, they should be prepared immediately, and the competent authorities of each province should check and consider the situation in each county and establish them as appropriate. 3. In order to cultivate the spirit of endurance and service, teachers and students should engage in actual farming. The number of workers in each agricultural farm should be limited to two, and the number of workers in each agricultural school should be limited to four. The agricultural farms and agricultural schools that have already been established should implement this principle from March of the 23rd year. 4. The General Outline of Implementation Principles for Political Education, Education Production, and Production Education, items 2, 3, and 4, are of great importance to production education and political reform. The work reports and inspection reports of each commissioner should be carefully examined and reported to the ministry item by item and section by section. The education and construction departments of each province should also examine the schools, factories, and agricultural farms at any time to see whether they are earnestly improving according to the general outline of principles, and report the improvement situation at any time. The above instructions are issued separately. This order is hereby issued to be obeyed and implemented, and to be instructed to be obeyed and implemented in a unified manner. The date of receipt shall be reported. This is a very important order."

Evolution of Private Universities Nationwide

The Ministry of Education has compiled statistics on the evolution of private universities nationwide. They are extracted as follows: (1) Soochow University was initially established by church members to expand church affairs by merging the Suzhou Bo Xi Academy and the Shanghai and Suzhou Chinese and Western Academies to form the current school. It officially opened in March of the 11th year of the Republic of China (1922) and was approved for registration in July of the 18th year (1929). (2) Aurora University was initially established by Cai Yuanpei and Ma Xiangbo because the Beijing Translation Academy was suspended due to the Wuxu coup. They consulted with the Society of Jesus to establish the current school. Departments were established year by year, and it was approved for registration in December of the 21st year of the Republic of China (1932). (3) Shanghai College was initially Shanghai Baptist University. In the 4th year of the Republic of China (1915), it was renamed Shanghai College and was approved for registration in March of the 18th year (1929). (4) Fudan University was initially the Fudan Public School organized by students of Aurora College. It was suspended during the Xinhai Revolution and resumed in the first year of the Republic of China (1912). The university department was established in the spring of the 11th year (1922), and it was approved for registration as Fudan University in October of the 17th year (1928). (5) Sino-French University was initially the Franco-Chinese Work-Study Association and the French Preparatory School organized by Chinese and foreign people in the World Society. In the 9th year (1920), it was renamed Sino-French University and was approved for registration in December of the 20th year (1931). (6) The University of Nanking was formed by merging the Huiwen and Hongyu Academies. In the 3rd year of the Republic of China (1914), the Oriental Medical College was also merged into the school. In July of the 10th year (1921), it was approved for registration by the former Ministry of Education. In September of the 17th year (1928), it was re-approved for registration by the University Council. (7) Tatung University was initially founded by the Lida Society and named Tatung College. In November of the 11th year (1922), it was approved for registration by the former Beijing Ministry of Education and renamed Tatung University. In September of the 17th year (1928), it was approved for registration by the former University Council. (8) Wuchang China University was established by Mr. Huangpi and others with donations. It was initially named China School. In the 2nd year of the Republic of China (1913), it was renamed University. In the 4th year (1915), it was approved for registration by the former Ministry of Education. It was suspended due to the political upheaval in September of the 15th year (1926). It was restored in February of the 17th year (1928) and was approved for registration in December of the 18th year (1929). (9) Lingnan University was initially the Gezhi Academy founded by an American. In the 12th year before the Republic of China (1900), it was renamed Lingnan School. In the 16th year of the Republic of China (1927), the Chinese took over and ran it independently, renaming it Lingnan University. It was registered in July of the 19th year (1930). (10) Cheeloo University The school was initially formed by merging the Guangwen School and the Jinan Cooperative Medical School and named with its present name. In the 12th year (1923), the Beijing North China Cooperative Women's School was also merged into the medical department of the school. In December of the 20th year (1931), it was approved for registration by the Ministry of Education. (11) (One) Yenching University was formed by the merger of North Tongzhou Cooperative University and Beijing Huiwen University. In the 9th year (1920), the Women's Cooperative was also merged in. In the spring of the 16th year (1927), it was recognized by the former Ministry of Education. In June of the 18th year (1929), it was approved for registration. (12) (Two) Nankai University was planned by Yan Fansun and others, the founders of Nankai School, in the winter of the 7th year of the Republic of China (1918). The university department was established in May of the 8th year (1919). It was recognized by the former Ministry of Education in the 14th year (1925), and approved for registration in June of the 18th year (1929). (13) (Three) Xiamen University was planned and founded by Chen Jiageng. In the 10th year of the Republic of China (1921), it was opened at Jimei School and was approved for registration in March of the 17th year (1928). (14) (Four) Amoy University was founded by students who left Xiamen University and professors such as Ou Yuanhuai. It was approved for registration in May of the 18th year (1929). (15) (Five) Wuchang Central China University was formed by the merger of the Department of Arts of Wuchang Wen Hua University, the Department of Arts of Bowen College, and the Yale University in Changsha, which were run by the church. It was suspended due to the political upheaval in the 16th year (1927). It was restored in the 18th year (1929) and Lakeview College was also merged in. In December of the 20th year (1931), it was approved for registration. (16) (Six) Kwang Hua University was founded by the parents of the students of St. John's University who left the school after the May 30th Massacre. It was approved for registration in May of the 18th year (1929). (17) (Seven) Guangdong National University was founded by private individuals and initially established a university department. Chen Zhongqu was publicly elected as the president. In October of the 14th year (1925), it was approved for registration by the Guangdong National Government. In July of the 20th year (1931), it was re-approved for registration, and the registration was retroactive to the 14th year (1925). (18) (Eight) Fu Jen Catholic University was a Catholic school. It was initially the Fu Jen Society and later renamed Fu Jen Catholic University. In June of the 16th year (1927), it was approved for trial operation by the Ministry. In August of the 20th year (1931), it was approved for registration. (19) (Nine) Guangzhou University was founded by private individuals such as Wu Zaimin. In August of the 16th year (1927), it was approved for establishment by the Guangdong National Government. In July of the 21st year (1932), it was approved for registration by the Ministry.

Fujian Education Circle Demands Back Payment of Old Debts from the Pseudo-Government, Chen Yi Considers it an Out-of-Line Action

| Out of Concern, the Annual Holiday is Abolished and Half a Month's Education Fees for February are Allocated in Advance |

After Zheng Zhenwen, the Director of the Fujian Education Department, took office in November of the 21st year (1932), he made extraordinary efforts in education facilities. During the rebellion of the rebellious army in Fujian, he left the province for Beijing to report the circumstances. The Central Government highly praised him for not joining the rebellion. Recently, after the rebellion was suppressed, he was re-appointed to the important position of Director of Education. The schools and social education institutions in Fujian also sent telegrams to the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Education, urging Mr. Zheng to return to the south as soon as possible. However, Mr. Zheng believed that the education funds of Fujian Province relied solely on salt tax revenue, but it was often affected by local unrest. Not only could new facilities not be gradually developed, but the original budget also faced difficulties. Unless special funds were determined, there would be no way to cope with it. He accompanied Commissioner Lin Zhiyuan to meet with the central financial and educational authorities, stating the suffering of the Fujian education circle and requesting relief measures. Finally, he drafted a report and presented it to Chairman Chen through whom it was submitted to Minister of Finance Kong for review. Minister Kong replied that the central government's finances were also difficult, and it was impossible to reissue old debts. From now on, the central government should allocate funds on a monthly basis, and education funds could be settled. After Mr. Zheng arrived in Fujian, he convened the principals of various schools and informed them of the negotiation process. He also led the principals to meet with Chairman Chen. The Chairman stated that under the current difficult financial situation, there were no funds to issue old debts. In the future, he would be responsible himself. He asked them to inform the faculty and staff to share the difficulties and try their best to maintain operations. However, the faculty and staff convened meetings for days, insisting that the old debts could not be cancelled, that 150% of the annual holiday fee should be paid, and threatened with a general strike. Chairman Chen was extremely furious upon hearing this. The education fee issue had been determined after several negotiations with the central government. Furthermore, the new provincial government was established on February 1st. How could the faculty and staff ask him to be responsible for the debts owed by Cheng Ren and the pseudo-government? Such an out-of-line behavior was extremely inappropriate and should be severely punished to serve as a warning to others. Out of concern, he specially ordered the Salt Affairs Inspection Branch Office to raise half a month's education fees for February in advance during the holiday. The responsible agency was responsible for collecting and distributing them separately.

Marek Discusses Danish and Chinese Civic Education in Beiping

▲ Danish Rural Civic Education Can Serve as a Reference for China

▲ Civic Education in Wuxi, Dingxian, and Beiping Has Gradually Developed

(Beiping Correspondence) After arriving in Beiping, Marek, the president of the Danish International People's College, lectured at Tsinghua University, Yenching University, and other schools, and was quite busy. The reporter specially visited Mr. Marek to inquire about the purpose of his visit to China and his impressions of visiting various places. Mr. Marek's replies were sincere. Today (the 8th) at 10:30 a.m., Marek lectured on Danish civic education in the eighth classroom of the Normal University, with the meaning focusing on higher civic education. The talks and lectures are recorded separately below.

Marek's Talk

After shaking hands with the reporter, Marek immediately made the following remarks: "I came to China to give lectures in various places and to take the opportunity to visit Chinese civic education. The Jiangsu Educational College in Wuxi has a well-organized structure, and the students' level is also high, similar to the higher folk high schools in Denmark. The Dingxian Mass Education Experiment Zone can indeed serve as a model mass education zone. There are many mass schools in Peiping. According to Chinese friends, there are more than one hundred mass schools in Peiping, which shows the development of mass education in China in recent years. However, Chinese mass education differs from Danish mass education in many respects. (1) Most of the Chinese mass schools are established by the government, while the Danish mass schools are all private. The government subsidizes the funds, but does not interfere with the school administration. (2) Chinese mass education focuses more on children's mass education, while Danish mass education focuses on working adult populations. China is an agricultural country, and Denmark is also an agricultural country. I hope that China and Denmark will join hands in the field of mass education in the future to jointly seek the universalization and practicalization of agricultural education. The staff of the Dingxian Mass Education Experiment Zone are very hardworking, and the equipment is also thorough. I hope that the staff will continue to work hard and seek further progress. Agricultural production in China has gone bankrupt in recent years. I hope that Chinese comrades, for the mass education in rural areas, regardless of official or private mass schools, will take into account the needs of the local environment and focus on agricultural arts or agricultural mass education. However, the Danish countryside is different from the Chinese countryside. Danish rural mass education can only be offered to China for reference. It is not necessary for Chinese rural mass schools to have the same facilities as Danish rural mass schools." I plan to stay in Peiping for a short time and then go to the United States and Canada to visit mass education, he said.

Danish Civic Education

Marek gave a lecture at 10:30 a.m. today (the 8th) in the eighth classroom of the Normal University, with more than 400 people attending. First, the president of the Normal University, Li Zheng, gave an introductory speech, followed by Marek's lecture in English on "Danish Civic Education," which was translated by Professor Chuan Baochen of the Normal University. It roughly stated that Chairman, Ladies and Gentlemen, I have come to your country from faraway Denmark. Today, I am very honored to have this opportunity to gather with you all. In Denmark, one-quarter of the farmers receive higher civic education. There are 51 farmer folk high schools, all of which are government-run. The government subsidizes the funds, but the school administration is not interfered with by the government. Most Danish farmers participate in general elections after graduating from higher folk high schools, so the level of Danish farmers is relatively high. Although Denmark's international status cannot reach the highest point, civic education has a considerable position in the international arena. Sweden, Norway, and Finland have also established folk high schools due to the influence of Danish civic education. Denmark has established the International People's College, which has been around for 13 years. There are usually 1,500 students, and the number of students in the winter short-term specialized courses increases to 2,000. Because farmers are more idle in winter, the number of students increases. Students from various countries study at the same school, understand each other, and students from various countries can obtain special materials from various countries, which is also a very interesting thing, he said. After the lecture, slides were shown, and the meeting adjourned at 12:30 p.m., he said.

Hangzhou City and Zhejiang University Jointly Hold a Teacher Training Workshop

▲ Workshops Will Be Held Once a Week from March to July

In order to promote the professional development of private primary school teachers in the city, the Hangzhou Municipal Government, in conjunction with the Department of Education of the Faculty of Arts and Sciences of Zhejiang University, will hold a teacher training workshop. The regulations of the association are excerpted as follows: (1) The Education Section of the Hangzhou Municipal Government, in order to promote the professional development of private primary school teachers in the city, in conjunction with the Department of Education of the Faculty of Arts and Sciences of Zhejiang University, will hold a teacher training workshop. (2) The number of students in this association is tentatively set at 100. (3) The training period of this association will be from March to July of the 23rd year, with one workshop per week, from 7:00 p.m. to 9:00 p.m. (4) The address of this association is the Faculty of Arts and Sciences of Zhejiang University on Daxue Road. (5) The subjects and workshop hours of this association are stipulated as follows: (1) Child guidance for 8 hours; (2) School administration for 6 hours; (3) Elementary school Chinese language teaching for 6 hours; (4) Elementary school arithmetic teaching for 6 hours; (5) Elementary school social studies for 6 hours; (6) Elementary school natural studies for 6 hours; (6) Elementary school health education for 6 hours; (8) Elementary school music education for 4 hours; (9) Elementary school art education for 4 hours; (10) Elementary school labor education for 6 hours; (10)(1) Elementary school combined teaching for 6 hours. Choose any five of the above subjects and decide at the time of registration. Changes are not allowed unless necessary. If the number of students joining each subject is less than ten, they may be incorporated into other subjects for listening. (6) In addition to the above subjects, Chinese, mathematics, nature, knowledge, and other subjects may be set up according to the needs of the students, but only if more than 40 students join can a class be opened, and the workshop hours will be determined at any time. (7) In addition to the stipulated workshop subjects, this association may hold special lectures at any time to increase students' interest. (8) Students should register with this association within three days of the start of registration. No more will be accepted after the quota is full. (9) Students who listen to the lecture for four-fifths of the time and pass the examination will be given prizes by this association. (10) The expenses of this association will be paid from the city's education funds.

Shanghai Japanese Correspondence School Enrollment

▲ Divided into Elementary, Advanced, and Translation Classes

He has authored three volumes of contemporary Japanese textbooks, as well as "Rapid Japanese Conversation" and "Japanese Correspondence," among others. The school is divided into three classes: elementary, advanced, and translation guidance. The elementary class is for beginners to learn pronunciation, with special methods employed, so learning pronunciation is not difficult at all. Its effectiveness is the same as direct listening. The advanced class studies literary works, advanced grammar, letter writing techniques, and conversation, etc. The translation guidance class specializes in guiding the translation of Japanese books and newspapers. Students can submit their trial translations for modification and correction. Enrollment for all classes has now begun. There are no qualifications required for students. Anyone interested in studying Japanese can enroll. Enrollment procedures and fees are detailed in the school's regulations. The regulations will be sent upon request. The school address is temporarily located at the Chinese Students' Bookstore, 552 Fourth Avenue, Shanghai. It is also reported that the professors employed by the school are all well-known figures in society, such as Zhang Ziping, Feng Cixing, and Zhou Xianwen, who have all been hired as responsible professors.

Zhou Deding's Mission to Inspect Education in Jiangsu and Zhejiang

Mr. Zhou Deding's trip to Jiangsu and Zhejiang to inspect social education is on behalf of the private Hunan Changsha suburban rural construction experimental area. It is not confirmed that he also represents the Hunan Provincial Department of Education, as rumored.

Special Report

Report on Vocational Education by a Ministry of Education Commissioner on Educational Inspection in Europe (13)

(1) Water and Forest School This school is managed by the Ministry of Agriculture and has a forest area of 3,450 hectares. Each hectare is 10,000 square meters, which is equivalent to slightly less than 20 mu in our country, making a total of approximately 38,000 mu. It has one principal, four professors, and two lecturers, with an administrative committee organization similar to a university, and also has one secretary-general and one director of affairs. Students are divided into two categories: (1) formal students, who are prospective government officials for water and forest administration, and (2) free students, who are foreign students and domestic students who attend lectures at will. In addition to teaching courses, professors also undertake research work. The basic subjects that students of each department should study are (1) biology, (2) botany, (3) zoology, and (4) soil properties, etc., applied to forests and waterways. In addition, there are practical mathematics, building construction, and forest regulations, forestry administration, etc. English and German are also taught as preparation for reading reference books. The academic year is divided into two semesters: winter is for studying theory, and summer is for practice. There is an examination once a year, and only those who pass can advance to the next grade. Forest research within the school is divided into four departments: 1. Research on forest production and climate; 2. Research on forest plants; 3. Research on forest animals; 4. Afforestation research. Research work in progress includes: 1. Soil: research on the acidity, alkalinity, and organization of other components of the soil; 2. Wood grain: the internal fiber texture of wood varies depending on the species of wood, and the differences are very obvious when viewed under a microscope; 3. Research on microorganisms in water; 4. Experiments on the load-bearing capacity of wood. The equipment is as follows: 1. Chemistry laboratory; 2. Botany laboratory; 3. Zoology laboratory; 4. Wood testing laboratory; 5. Botanical garden. The school collects specimens in the following departments: 1. Tree specimens, from France and abroad; 2. Forest game; 3. Forest beasts; 4. Fish in French rivers; 5. Fossil specimens; 6. Mineral specimens; 7. Soil specimens. Soil specimens from all over France are on display for research, stored in small square cabinets, about one meter high. The soil quality gradually changes its organization, color, and viscosity from the ground up, which is clear at a glance.

The areas of the French Alps and Pyrenees mountains, where plants could not grow in the past, have been studied and transformed by the school, and have been transformed into lush forests in sixty years.

Lyon

1. Industrial Chemistry School This school was originally a private school subsidized by the government, but recently it has been entirely maintained by private chemical manufacturers, but it is affiliated to the university administration. Most of the school's directors are industrialists. The president of the University of Lyon is also one of the directors. The academic program is divided into three years, as follows: first year - inorganic chemistry and analysis; second year - organic chemistry; third year - (first semester) applied chemistry, (second semester) dyes, perfumes, electrochemistry, and microbiology, leather making.

Emphasis is placed on experimental work, so there is a lot of practical work. Students entering the school do not need to be graduates of higher middle schools who have obtained a baccalaureate, but they must pass an entrance examination. The laboratory and equipment are spacious and well-equipped. Professors all have research rooms.

(2) Leather Making School This school has been established for forty years. When it was founded, the leather making industry was still very immature. There were no experts or books. Now it has gradually achieved results. The academic program is divided into three years. In the first two years, students learn general chemistry and principles. In the third year, emphasis is placed on leather making practice. Professors also do a lot of research work. The school's organization is similar to that of the Industrial Chemistry School. The board of directors is also composed of representatives of factory owners. The government does not provide subsidies, only acts as an advisor and supervisor.

(3) Central Engineering School This school is a private engineering school. Its organization is similar to a joint-stock company. The board of directors is responsible for planning the economy. The academic program is divided into four years. The first year is a preparatory course, so the regular course is only three years. Students entering the school must pass an examination. Those who directly take the regular course must first obtain an advanced mathematics certificate. In the first and second years of the regular course, students must obtain three certificates: (1) General Mathematics Certificate, (2) General Physics Certificate, and (3) Mechanics Certificate, before they can enter the third year.

The third year is divided into three departments: 1. Civil Engineering

General Civil Engineering

2. Mechanical Engineering Mech Engineering

Electrical Technique

The professors are all current engineers, so students get practical knowledge.

(4) National Vocational School This school is divided into two departments: (1) Higher Elementary School, (2) National Vocational School. The courses taught are also divided into general education and practical arts courses. The arts courses are metalwork, foundry work, model making, woodwork, industrial design, instrument design, watchmaking, etc. In the advanced commercial class, literature, accounting, stand and English, German, Italian, or Spanish are also taught.

The academic program is divided into four years. The daily study hours are from eight to ten hours. The weekly practical work is 32 hours, and the theoretical study is 20 hours. After four years of graduation, only those who pass the examination will be awarded a certificate. If students of this school want to go to a higher vocational school, they must add preparatory subjects for further education in the third and fourth years, such as mathematics and physics. Additional training is required to ensure connection. However, these students who want to further their education must be the best in the class. Most of the teachers are current engineering personnel or have sufficient experience. Tuition is free. Students at this school must pay 2,400 francs for all board and lodging expenses. The practical factories are divided into the following types: (1) Woodworking model, (2) Sand casting, (3) Forging, (4) Metalworking, (5) Not clear, (6) Clock and watch factory. The following characteristics of professors are noteworthy: (1) In the sand casting practice class, the shortcomings of students' work are clearly pointed out and displayed in a special place for public criticism and recognition; (2) In the forging and blacksmithing department, each practical work must first be given to students with a blueprint, and the steps from raw materials to finished products in each stage are marked on the blueprint, so that students can follow the blueprint and gradually advance, which is very clear. In recent years, France has often combined elementary and higher schools with national vocational schools in one school. The former emphasizes general education, while the latter pays attention to arts and crafts training, and the level is the same. Therefore, students can transfer from one department to another according to their interests, which is an aid to employment guidance and a new trend in French education.

(4) British Vocational Education

At the beginning of its development, education at all levels in Britain relied heavily on the efforts of private individuals and public groups. This was true for secondary education and primary education, and it was also true for vocational education. When we read the history of British vocational education, we can see that in Britain at that time, industry and commerce were already highly developed, and it still took so long to achieve results, which shows that vocational education is not easy to promote. The motivation for British vocational education was the 1851 Industrial Exhibition, which made people aware of the importance of science applied to industry and commerce. Therefore, in 1853, the Department of Science and Art was established, which belonged to the Ministry of Commerce. The government allocated special funds to encourage schools teaching science. The department was responsible for the overall success, and the amount of the bonus depended on the students' achievements. However, the scope of the bonus was limited to natural sciences, and did not include industrial education. In 1880, the London Trades Association was established, and the trades associations collected money to subsidize engineering subjects, and industrial education was thus blessed and made progress day by day. For more than fifty years, with the government's advocacy and incentives, and the efforts of public groups, British vocational education has become a grand sight. Technical colleges are all founded by private individuals. Their initial purpose is to integrate morality, physical fitness, and group activity as the foundation of training, to be an educational institution and a place for self-cultivation. Administrative affairs are presided over by a committee, and the London Municipal Committee must have a considerable number of representatives participating in the affairs. In order to avoid duplication in subjects, the technical colleges all agree in advance to teach certain engineering subjects, such as mechanical engineering and electrical engineering, as one category, chemical engineering as one category, and architectural engineering as another category. Each is undertaken by one technical college or several colleges. This is the general situation. Most junior industrial and commercial schools are attached to technical colleges, but vocational schools for women are still mostly separated.

Industrial schools, established by the London Municipal Committee, are mostly specialized in nature, such as printing schools and architectural schools, but there are also multi-disciplinary schools. The management rights are all in the hands of the Municipal Committee, and part of the administrative duties are delegated to the advisory committee of each school by the Municipal Education Committee, which is responsible for handling them.

Supplementary Schools Supplementary education can be divided into two categories: one is supplementary vocational subjects, and the other is supplementary general education. The academic level is quite uneven. Supplementary vocational subjects are the most important work in the current vocational education system in Britain. All advanced classes and specialized classes of industrial schools are included. These subjects are mostly taught in evening classes, but the engineering and construction industries sometimes allow their employees to attend classes during the day, but this is still a minority. General supplementary subjects are divided into day classes and evening classes, which are designed for employees and workers to continue their primary school education and supplement their general knowledge.

National Certificate Examination One of the most special points in British vocational education, which is not found in other European countries, is the national certificate examination at all levels. This examination is divided into two categories: the first category is the certificate examination, and the second category is the diploma examination, and each category is further divided into advanced and specialized types. Both the certificate and diploma examinations require three or two years of study in a technical college or vocational school before one can participate. The right to award certificates and diplomas is controlled by the Ministry of Education and the Engineers Association. For example, when a technical college establishes a mechanical engineering certificate course, it must first submit the plan to the Ministry of Education and the Mechanical Engineers Association. The two institutions will conduct a detailed examination. If the mechanical equipment is well-equipped, the teachers are qualified, and the curriculum and teaching materials are appropriate, then the establishment of the course is allowed. Other certificate or diploma courses, such as electrical engineering and chemical engineering, must also go through the same procedures when they are established. There are now five types that have been approved for establishment: mechanical engineering, electrical engineering, shipbuilding engineering, chemical engineering, and architectural engineering, which have been jointly reviewed and approved by the Ministry of Education and the five engineering associations.

The curriculum of each subject is divided into supplementary classes and specialized classes. The subjects of each course are prescribed in advance and are called joint subjects. For example, the general engineering course combines mechanical drawing, applied mechanics, mathematics, and other subjects into joint subjects. For electrical engineering, the joint subjects are electrical principles, mathematics, mechanics, mechanical drawing, electrical design, and electrical transportation. The organization and distribution of the joint subjects for other chemical and mechanical engineering courses are roughly similar. The teaching materials for supplementary classes are slightly simpler and are called supplementary joint subjects. The level of specialized classes is higher and is called specialized joint subjects. Those who study in supplementary classes are only given certificates, and those who study in specialized classes are given diplomas. Certificates and diplomas are divided into ordinary and advanced types. Students who are 14 or 15 years old when they enter school, or who have studied in junior vocational schools for more than two years, can enter advanced supplementary classes. The course is three years long, and at least 150 hours of instruction must be provided each year (the minimum limit for chemical engineering courses is 180 hours per year). There are three evening classes each week. Those who pass the graduation examination are given ordinary certificates. Students who are older and have a higher level, and who study in specialized supplementary classes, have a course of two years. Those who pass the graduation examination are given advanced certificates.

Those who study in specialized classes, if they enter advanced specialized classes, are given ordinary diplomas after graduation. Those who enter specialized specialized classes are given advanced diplomas. The course length is at least three years (the Chemical Engineers Association only gives certificates and does not give diplomas because the students' results are not good).

Disappointment in Expectations for Foreign Cotton, Bullish Traders Exit the Market

▲ Cotton to Be Calculated in Catties Starting in July

The cotton market fell sharply, and the bearish trend intensified. Due to last year's sharp rise, most people expected that foreign cotton would continue to rise during the holiday. During this holiday, US cotton did not move, while Indian cotton rose slightly by 3 to 4 rupees. However, with the exchange rate rising, the calculated price per dan fell by one yuan compared to last year, and people's confidence weakened. Ningbo bullish traders exited the market with 20,000 dan. However, the intention of the large number of bullish traders remains firm. However, there is still no flaw in foreign cotton.

Zheng Standard Plummets by More Than One Yuan

In the pre-market session of Zheng Standard, bullish traders liquidated in large quantities, and market prices suddenly loosened. Prices for each month fell by 1.10 yuan to 1.05 yuan. At the noon closing, near-month contracts rebounded by 5 cents, and far-month contracts were flat. The total turnover for the day was 159,700 dan. The sales by various firms were: Changhe 8,400 dan, Yifeng 5,400 dan, Changfeng 3,600 dan, Yuanxingchang 11,000 dan, Gengfeng 7,200 dan, Chunji 5,900 dan, Hengyi 3,300 dan, Dafeng 2,800 dan, Yongchang 2,200 dan. The purchases were: Dachang 6,100 dan, Xincheng 6,800 dan, Shenchang 4,100 dan, Yichang 7,100 dan, Taichang 3,800 dan, Renfeng 3,600 dan, Shenyu 5,300 dan, Ruida 3,100 dan, Huikang 7,200 dan, Yuanda 2,000 dan. Grain Market Suspended, Actual Sales Stagnant

Flour Prices Continue to Fall

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning, the market prices for each month showed a uniform downward trend. After a suspension of more than ten days, the price of foreign wheat, although there was no huge fluctuation, the actual sales appetite in Canada remained weak. The flour taken by the large bullish traders in the previous month was mostly still in their hands, and this month is also a flat month. Counting the official trading days, there are less than ten days, and all futures must be settled. In addition, the price of spot foreign wheat in Argentina has loosened, and it is only calling for 4.15 yuan. Therefore, after the opening price, the market atmosphere was not stable. Then, Fuxin and Fufeng factories all had to sell to cope with the situation, and the market situation stepped downstream again. There were few new bullish traders, and old bullish traders also returned to the market, so the downward trend became more violent. As a result, the flour for this month fell by 3.5 cents before the market closed, March fell by 4 cents, April fell by 3.5 cents, May fell by 3 cents, June fell by 2.5 cents, and July fell by 3.25 cents.

New Wheat Standard Likely to Enter Customs at 3 Yuan

| Affected by Rice Prices |

Yesterday, after the opening of the wheat futures market in the morning and afternoon, the market for each month, the recent period saw very little trading due to a lack of buyers and sellers. March only opened in the morning, priced at 4.0275 yuan, which was about 8 or 9 cents lower than before the market closed. June opened at 3.755 yuan in both the morning and afternoon, also down 8 or 9 cents. As for the new goods for July, the selling was very strong, partly because the weather was very good, and partly because the spot goods in Argentina were very cheap, so people's hearts were uniformly weak, and the downward trend was very strong, falling by a huge 1.2 cents compared to before the market closed. According to speculation by people in the industry, due to the low price of rice, the new standard may enter customs at 3 yuan, which is also possible. The current wheat has no market due to the guild, and only the packages have not been opened.

Rice Market Sees a Significant Improvement on the Red Board

(South Shanghai) The Red Board situation: the sources for each syndicate after the big year-end settlement last year, the successive arrivals at the port totaled more than 130 boatloads (more than 16,000 shi), of which the thick japonica rice from various syndicates accounted for the majority, and the late rice and various colors accounted for half. The sales markets in various regions were quite lively at the beginning of the year. Each syndicate's appetite could not be fully satisfied. The opening of the Red Board was much better than last year. For example, the thick japonica rice from Chang Syndicate, Su Syndicate, and South Port Syndicate increased by half a cent, and the late rice such as Qingjiao, Songsi, and Xilian each increased by an unusual amount. However, Dubu pointed rice and various colors were slightly mixed, rising by 10 to 20 cents or several points.

(North Shanghai) The eight-day Spring Festival holiday has ended. There are 60 to 70 boats in stock and arriving in He Xia. The sales appetite for each type of goods is all for social purposes, so it is very light. The opening prices for each type of goods are higher than the closing price by a cent, the price of white japonica thin rice is higher by a cent, the price of Yangbu pointed rice is higher by 2 cents, and the price of Ke pointed rice is higher by nearly a cent. The price of Yin Yuan and Bai Yuan is stable.

Various Syndicates' Attitudes Towards the Trading of Foreign Indica Rice

▲ Foreign Indica Rice Changed to 180 Catties Per Dan

Yesterday, the market for foreign Indica rice on the Red Board was not very prosperous. This was because each syndicate was cautious and unwilling to sell and buy boldly. Moreover, the opening of accounts by the silver and money industry was pending, and the roots had not yet circulated. Quanzhou Syndicate originally had an appetite, but due to the exchange rate and silver root, there was no movement yesterday. Fuzhou Syndicate was slightly more accommodating, but not very active, and tens of thousands of bags had been shipped last winter, and the local needs were now sufficient. Ningbo Syndicate has a strong digestion, but it shipped 35,000 bags of foreign rice Indica rice at the end of last winter, and there is no need for it now. Therefore, only the local street and Min Sheng Yuan Syndicate purchased a total of 2,000 bags plus a small amount. The inventory of Indica rice is very abundant, but the owners do not want to sell lightly because the cost is high, and foreign rice has actually been taxed, and the taxation in Fujian Province will also be implemented in the coming days. Therefore, although the trading volume is small, the market remains strong. The small twisted foreign rice is up by 5 points compared to last winter, which is the reason for the foreign rice tax. The Fujian Syndicate purchased 242 bags of Hunan oil, priced at 7.5 yuan, 600 bags of unpolished oil, priced at 6.3 yuan, 750 bags of Mingguang Indica rice, priced at 6.85 yuan to 6.7 yuan, 155 bags of Nanjing Liu Indica rice, priced at 6.1 yuan, the local street purchased 76 bags of Jiangxi red late rice, priced at 7.1 yuan, 100 bags of Hunan machine oil, priced at 7.5 yuan, Jing 100 bags, priced at 6.3 yuan, Jing unpolished 150 bags, priced at 5.53 yuan, and 200 bags of small twisted rice were returned goods, priced at 6.85 yuan.

Since the implementation of the new measurement in this city, He Xia rice has long been changed to the city dou, but foreign Indica rice has not been changed due to customs reporting. Now that the customs have complied with the change, the grain industry has received instructions from the Municipal Social Bureau to change it. Therefore, from yesterday, each dan of foreign Indica rice has been changed to 180 catties by city scale, but calculated according to the old rules, it is still the same.

Miscellaneous Grains Lack Upward Momentum

Spot miscellaneous grains officially opened yesterday, and market prices were all sold according to the whole city scale. The Red Board trading was still good, but the market conditions still lacked upward momentum. Yesterday, soybeans were traded by Fuzhou Syndicate and the local street. The factory did not move. A total of 13 or 14 cartloads of various beans were traded in the city. Market prices were high, flat, and secondary fixed. Green beans are colored goods, and the market conditions have not been insulted. Yesterday, 700 bags of Guide green beans were purchased from the interior. The local street purchased 250 bags of Dalian mixed green beans. Sand yellow Du beans were flat. Broad beans were opened for 600 to 700 bags of Ningbo goods, which were digested by Fuzhou Syndicate and foreign merchants. Market prices were quite stable. Green beans, Guang Syndicate, Little Luzon Syndicate, and Xiamen Syndicate all inquired. The total city traded 1,700 or 1,800 bags of bright and raw green beans. The market shape is temporarily stable. Sesame market prices have not changed much. Guang Syndicate purchased more than 700 bags of white sesame. Xiamen Syndicate purchased 42 bags of black sesame. Raw kernels are still weaker than peanuts.

Oil Market, Oil Cakes Red Board Not Prosperous

The Red Board market for soybean oil and peanut oil, because each firm had stocks in hand at the time of closing, and sales households in various places have not yet been listed, so most of the goods traded yesterday were social transactions. Market prices were 20 to 30 cents lower than at the time of closing. The decline in soybean cakes was even more severe, with a difference of 5 points compared to the closing market. The reason is that there has been no news from the mainland, and exports have been hit by direct transportation, and the market conditions are not prosperous.

North and South Goods, Daylily Suddenly Rises by Two Yuan on the Red Board

| Black Dates and Walnuts Also Tend to Rise |

Daylily, because the stock of each firm is thin, and the various markets in Zhenjiang have not opened, the goods in Shanghai have also been pulled up. It is heard that only hundreds of bags were traded in the first session yesterday, with prices such as Daxing vegetables at 19.8 yuan and Township Village vegetables at 18.8 yuan, which is more than 2 yuan higher than before the Spring Festival. Judging from this situation, the future market is still expected to rise. The firms, in view of the flexibility of the sales channels of various syndicates, are also holding on tightly. Black dates and walnuts, because the sources have been scarce for a long time, and the stock is also sparse, the market prices have risen. For example, hand-picked peaches are 20 yuan, Shimen peaches are 18.5 yuan, Changping peaches are 18 yuan, Yanggu peaches are 17 yuan, Gaozhuang Yuan dates are from 15 yuan to 18 yuan, and black dates are 11 yuan to 12 yuan.

Sugar Market, Coarse Sand White Returns Fall by 5 Cents

| Five Fortunes Wen Bing Rises by 20 to 30 Cents |

Yesterday, the sugar market, because the price of gold turned down, the guild's disk, such as the 24th coarse sand white return, fell by a small 5 cents, to 19.95 yuan. Transactions were still rare. Transshipment high ordinary goods were 6.8 yuan, No. 9 Dutch red was 15.95 yuan, No. 8 and 9 Dutch red was 15.7 yuan, and Chaoqing was not open because the sales channels of various syndicates had not moved. Dozens of bags of Mianbai were opened, priced at 20.05 yuan. Zhiyang was 16.05 yuan. The factory's white fell by 10 cents, to 19.1 yuan. The Jianbing number plate only came from the Dalaiahua number plate, which opened more than 100 boxes of Wufu Wenbing, priced at 18.3 yuan per pile, which was 20 to 30 cents higher than before the Spring Festival. Hainan red flakes and green flakes have not yet been opened.

Free Talk

Prophecy

— Xu Maoyong

Now, even the Chinese believe that this world cannot but change. Because they believe it will change, they want to know how it will change, so everyone loves to hear prophecies. Many magazine companies have therefore specifically created topics and asked people to make predictions. But those they invited are all people who specialize in writing articles, or, to put it nicely, intellectuals.

Originally, there was a specific type of person who made prophecies. China had astrologers, and foreign countries also had so-called prophets. They relied on "divine will" or "inspiration." But modern people no longer believe them much. What modern people believe are the predictions of intellectuals, because they make comprehensive observations based on objective facts and then deduce the inevitable "fruit" from the established "cause." This is more scientific, so everyone believes them, and they make predictions with great certainty.

However, the predictions of intellectuals still rarely have accuracy. Because the observation and reasoning abilities of intellectuals are fundamentally subject to various limitations. For example, the observation of an intellectual of the bourgeoisie can only be detailed in the affairs of the bourgeoisie, and the deduction is only based on the standpoint of the bourgeoisie. The affairs and fate of other classes will inevitably be ignored. Needless to say, such predictions are not very reliable.

Moreover, when intellectuals make deductions based on scientific methods, no matter how rigorous and solemn their arguments and reasoning are, they can never escape the concept of gradual change. If the changes in society were always gradual, then the predictions of intellectuals might be correct by chance. However, changes in society are actually often sudden. This sudden change is not without a "cause," but the existence of its "cause" is originally obscure and not easily seen by the general public. The general public only sees some obvious "causes" and deduces the future "fruit" based on this, but they do not know that the future "fruit" is often determined by potential "causes," beyond the expectations of the prophets.

For example, when talking about World War II, most prophets believed that it would occur in 1936. But what would happen after it occurred? The prophets could not explain it. Aside from imagining how bombers would destroy cities and how poison gas would take lives, they could not think of any other results. Such predictions make the public despair and thus cultivate a passive concept of fatalism. On the other hand, it makes people in the morbid state of the end of the century feel excited by the great stimulation, which in turn promotes the realization of war. This kind of prophecy is very harmful.

World war is indeed a crisis of destruction, but if a kind of power accidentally erupts among the masses of the world, it may not be possible to turn danger into safety and make it a turning point for a new life. Some may think that "chance" is too uncertain, but in fact, there is no so-called chance in the development of history. What is accidental is just the necessity that we have never seen. Moreover, it is the masses who create history. In the past, the chaos of the masses made the darkness last for a long time. In the future, the awakening of the masses will surely make the light appear suddenly. And the awakening of the masses is not a hopeless thing, so we do not need to despair of the crises that today's prophets are flaunting.

Overseas Remembrances of a Poetic Soul

— Luo Ailan

——Mourning Zhu Xiang

Ziyuan, this morning I was reading a newspaper in the Columbia Chinese Library when I unintentionally read the news of your suicide in the Yangtze River. Ziyuan, are you really no longer among the living? Or am I dreaming? But the words on the newspaper were vivid and real, and the room was full of sunlight, how could this be a dream?

From the sparse hundred-odd words in the newspaper, I can see that the reason for your suicide was poverty. Alas, Ziyuan, you should have understood that society simply cannot accommodate poets, and the masses are the executioners of genius. It is your misfortune to be a poet, and even more unfortunate to be a genius poet. Even if you didn't commit suicide, society and the masses would still want to kill you.

Some people will say that your suicide was an act of weakness, but such people simply do not understand you and are just echoing what others say. If you were truly weak, you would have humbled yourself to survive, you would have wagged your tail and begged for mercy, and you would never have dared to topple [redacted] great idols for the sake of art and truth, or used toilet paper to write letters to denounce [redacted] once extremely popular editor. If you hadn't offended these academic authorities, literary giants, and their minions, you might now be sitting pretty, perhaps as a dean or director of some university. However, you didn't, you preferred poverty, you preferred suicide. Could someone without courage do such a thing?

Ziyuan, although society mistreated poets, the works of poets remain in the world forever. Your body may have disappeared forever with the waves of the great river, but your complete personality remains forever in the hearts of your friends, and your poems and writings will shine forever, as eternal as the sun and moon. Ziyuan, thinking of this, you should be smiling in the afterlife!

However, your death means that I have lost a good companion in the anti-Friends group, and a bright star has fallen in the literary world. This sorrow is forever difficult to dispel, and this loss is forever impossible to make up.

Genius is rare in the world, and it is even rarer to find genius who can cherish themselves, work hard, and be faithful to art. Ziyuan, you have gone to eternal sleep, what more can we say!

Translation and Introduction

— Ren Baige

I have always thought this way: rather than piecing together a so-called original essay by plagiarizing from here and there, it is better to honestly translate the original works separately in order to fulfill the responsibility of introducing them. Of course, this does not mean that I am belittling original creation. In fact, plagiarism can also be said to be an introduction, and perhaps it is more suitable for those who only seek something that is easy to read and understand. However, someone who is truly dedicated to learning will likely say impolitely: this is not acceptable.

After all, because there are too few people who can speak impolitely, this trend continues to be popular. From partial plagiarism to complete appropriation, this was already quite remarkable, but recently many more variations have emerged: some take the approach of commenting on ancient books, copying other people's articles piece by piece, adding a bit of commentary at the end that can be considered their own opinion, and presenting it as an article; others translate the entire article, put their own name in the author's position, and relegate the original author's name to the back of the article to hide. This is naturally much more sophisticated than simply copying and appropriating, mainly because it leaves a retreat that they believe is very safe.

It is said that in the West, when translating famous works, the translator's name is often not signed, so that the original author's status is not taken away by the translator. From this, it can be seen that this kind of practice is probably rarely seen in "foreign" and "ancient" times, but is unique to "Chinese" and "modern" times. I think everyone knows its value and fate, so there is no need for me to say more.

However, this leaves us with a problem that we cannot ignore: it is absolutely impossible to do as they do in the West and not sign the translator's name. The reason is very simple, to use an old saying, "It is permissible to have the ambition of Yi Yin, but to usurp without the ambition of Yi Yin is wrong." For example, a few years ago, when the trend of translation was once popular, a batch of clumsy translations for which no one was responsible, or seemingly many people were responsible, appeared on the market. It is said that these were things rushed out by several people working together for fear of being preempted, and as a result, no one dared to take responsibility, so they had to publish them without names or under pseudonyms. This kind of translation will naturally drag good things into the mud as well, so it finally ruined the entire translation industry. "Realizing that the past cannot be retrieved, knowing that the future can be pursued," can the Chinese cultural world withstand another such disaster and loss?

Now, because it is even more difficult to speak out, many opinions often have to be borrowed from other people's mouths, and many people are already proposing to accept the legacy of literature. Perhaps in the near future, translation will raise its head again. However, I hope first of all that it will not only be a timely piece of writing, but will become the beginning of a great work. Furthermore, it should generate many real and powerful things from "faithful introduction," "systematic introduction," and "critical introduction." Only in this way can it be said that we are truly accepting the "legacy."

Whether a nation can properly accept the culture of progress is the same as whether a person can listen to good advice. This can determine its fate and future. Will we let ourselves perish or grow?

Birth

— Xiuhu

This day, he wrote in his diary:——

× month × day In the early morning, around five o'clock, a man and a woman were slowly moving forward on the deserted road. The woman was crying out in pain, and the man supported her as she stood. After a while, they slowly moved forward again, speaking softly to each other, and sometimes even showing a smile. Those were me and Jinzhen. Jinzhen had started labor at three o'clock and was about to give birth. There were no cars nearby, and it was late at night, so we couldn't see any rickshaws either. We had no choice but to support her as we walked and waited for a car to take her to the hospital.

At two o'clock in the afternoon, outside the door of Delivery Room No. 2 at the Red Cross Hospital, there was a man wearing a white coat like a doctor, with a white towel on his head, standing there anxiously, pacing back and forth, and peeking through the crack in the door from time to time. That was me.

A terrible scream came from the delivery room, which really made me anxious and restless. But this sound soon subsided. I looked through the crack in the door and saw her head lying crookedly on the operating table, her face covered with a piece of gauze. The doctor was performing surgery next to her with a scalpel. She had probably been anesthetized and passed out. I recalled the scene of her writhing in pain that I had just witnessed in the room, and I still couldn't help but shudder.

Although I had heard a lot about the pain of childbirth, how could I truly feel it unless I had experienced it myself? I remember the Japanese writer Hakuson Kuriyagawa comparing the birth of a new era to the pain of childbirth. The former is the struggle for human survival, while the latter is the struggle for human continuation of life. The two have the same value in the meaning of life. Both are equally arduous struggles. However, a hero who struggles for the era is often praised by all mankind, while women, who bear half of the arduousness of life, are still under oppression and are not cared for. Why is this?

If it is said that mankind created its own history, then on the credit book of creation, women alone bear half of the heavy responsibility of history because they produce the people who continue this historical creation.

At 2:50, the child was born. I saw through the crack in the door that the doctor was holding a grayish-white baby upside down. The body still had bloodstains from the mother's body. I couldn't help but faint, holding onto the door frame, trembling non-stop. This is a child, a flesh and blood separated from me and her? It was as if I had never thought about it before, that between us, there would be such a new life appearing before my eyes.

I immediately realized: this is my child, I am now a father. I immediately felt love for him. Yes, I will love him, I will work harder, for his happiness, for the happiness of all mankind. He should become the most complete member of society. Because he is a child of the new era, he bears a greater and more distant historical mission than I do. Jinzhen and I produced him, and in his hands, he will produce a new era.

The child cried, this was the first sound he made when he was born into the world. I hurried to check the time, it was 2:50.

I returned from the stairwell to the door of the delivery room, passing a ward, which was full of people, and some were crying. A patient there had just breathed their last and died. In the same minute, one person was born in the world, and another person died. The hospital is truly a dividing line of life. Some are born here, and some die here. The iron law of human metabolism is being played out on this line. My child represents the new, and that person represents the old.

At the door of the delivery room, I met the midwife, who told me that it was a "sister." I couldn't help but think immediately: "Many years later, she will be like her mother, perhaps lying in the same room, on the same bed, giving birth to the next generation."

The world is a river, and life is the flowing water in between. This child is just beginning to come into the world like flowing water.

I Curse Your Smile (6)

— Wu Yan

"It's really strange! He wants a woman from me… What women do I have! … I don't run a brothel! …"

"They just want those Baiyi girls…"

The boss pointed with his mouth to the rooms where the guests were sleeping, saying softly, acting like he understood everything. Then he added a sentence, meaning that I should be sensible and not show such an ugly face in front of the distinguished guests.

"We can't afford to offend them… These are people sent by the Bamu officials to inspect the roads… Opening a shop here, sigh, it's really…"

He didn't continue, sighing in distress.

I suppressed my anger and softened my voice slightly, saying:

"Are you asking me to take him to find one…"

The boss nodded.

But I said with a lot of aversion:

"I can't do such a thing, I can't, I can't, I can't… I don't understand Baiyi language… Wouldn't it be better to ask the landlady?"

The last sentence was almost said with gritted teeth.

"Hmm, hmm, what are you saying! What are you saying!…"

The boss immediately lost his temper. He grabbed the flashlight in the foreigner's hand and stammered:

"Come, come… Sir, I, I'll take you, I'll take you."

Immediately, a painful realization, like a bullet, shot into my heart; could I really watch those poor Yi girls being abused? Looking at the sleeping Indian, he didn't say anything at all, just closed his eyes and shook his blue chin. He, like my boss, was trapped in a helpless situation.

Useless fellows! I cursed viciously in my heart, and at the same time, a flame of hatred ignited. I didn't want to do the unlucky job of sweeping horse manure and serving guests anymore. Tonight, I would give that foreign devil a good beating, and run back to China that night or the next morning. But thinking about leaving the trouble to this family and that Indian, I couldn't bear it. Moreover, it would put my three poor little students into the mouth of the tiger, which made me even more uncomfortable. Because they were too innocent, they never treated me like a shop assistant, but always respected and loved me like a teacher. However, could I close my eyes and let those Yi girls who were struggling hard in life be ravished? That was impossible for me! Absolutely impossible! So, I suddenly chased after the boss and that foreign devil.

But I didn't raise my fist, but only grabbed the flashlight in the boss's hand and said urgently:

"I'll do it!"

"Hmm, hmm…"

The boss still looked very dissatisfied, but he didn't say anything. He handed the flashlight to me and quickly turned away. The way he looked was as if he was saying, if you can't get along with those Baiyi girls and you make a fuss, that's none of my business because this is what you volunteered to do.

So, this embarrassing and unpleasant job was all placed on my shoulders. But at this time, my heart was very calm, because the plan to deal with the matter had already been laid out in my mind in an instant. Walking to the door of the room where those Baiyi girls were sleeping, I suddenly stopped, stood in front of the foreign devil, and asked quietly:

"What do you want?"

The intention was to make him a little angry, deliberately pretending not to understand.

"I want a girl—deauful girlo"

Supplement to Shenbao Local News

Talking Points

One-Sentence Comments

— Fei Ren

Since occupying the Northeast, Japan has been frantically preparing for war, undertaking large-scale construction projects, and building railways and the South Manchuria Railway, causing friction when it is in a difficult situation.

(Note) This is called asking for trouble.

Zhuang Jingke, a Fujianese who once held important positions such as ambassador to Japan and governor of Zhili Province, was suddenly shot and killed by a young man at his private residence on Fukushima Street in the Japanese concession on the eve of the abolished lunar New Year.

(Note) This is called killing a chicken to warn the monkey.

The puppet emperor will proclaim himself emperor next month, and recently sent Pan and Zhang secretly to Tianjin to prepare to contact traitors and hold a celebration.

(Note) This is purely a shameful act.

An electrical dispatch from Changchun on the 18th stated that thousands of righteous soldiers in the east of Heilongjiang twice defeated the Japanese army, and Sergeant Oshima was killed in battle.

(Note) This shows that the people's hearts have not completely died out.

British commercial representatives in Tokyo urged Japan to be self-aware, pointing out that it will become the world's public enemy.

(Note) I am afraid that Japan will not realize this until its death.

In the case of Qian Shaofeng avenging his father's death, the lawyer defended Qian, roughly saying that the defendant was filial and courageous and should be given a light sentence.

(Note) This is truly a good son.

In the bribery case of Japanese Minister of Education Hatoyama, the Ministry of Justice ignored it, and Hatoyama, in order to save face, resigned around the 21st.

(Note) The political morality of Japan can be seen from this.

The rent reduction movement is expanding day by day, and many foreigners have joined it.

(Note) This is not a small problem, but a serious problem that deserves attention.

During the Gregorian New Year, all sectors showed no interest, but during the abolished Lunar New Year, the people were busy celebrating the New Year and were particularly interested.

(Note) This shows the greatness of our people's "conservatism" and "worship of antiquity."

Britain and France held frank talks to find a compromise method for military reduction.

(Note) I don't think there is any way to find one here.

The King of Belgium died while mountain climbing, and all of Europe mourned.

(Note) Truly a good king.

The supervisor of the Zizhu Grove in Lingyin Temple in Hangzhou accused the abbot of not only soliciting donations but also slandering him, so he hired lawyer Fan Ming to file a lawsuit against Mingjing in the First Special District Court for defamation.

(Note) This is truly looking for black-hearted people to eat vegetarian food.

Street Hero

— Daini

On New Year's Eve, with a worried face, I must shake and swagger out on the first day of the New Year to enjoy myself, otherwise, it seems that I am letting down this annual New Year's Day (now it is said that there are two). I didn't have anyone coming to my door with lanterns on New Year's Eve, so I am naturally even more different from everyone else on the first day of the New Year. I don't burn incense at the City God Temple, but I have to take a look at the New Year's atmosphere. Embracing the feeling that I have aged another year, I confidently walk out of the door like an old man. But "slap" a sound startled me from behind. Looking back, several children above the age of children burst out laughing. Yes, firecrackers. The few copper coins deducted from debts on New Year's Eve are not enough to play a round of pai gow. It is more economical to set off a few firecrackers, not to mention that scaring people is a way of entertaining that harms others and does not benefit oneself. I can't remember my childhood. I don't know if I have ever wasted my New Year's money like this, no, amused myself. Now, because I think of myself as an old man, and it is the first day of the New Year, I should get some good luck. But shouting and scolding as soon as I walk out of the door will not get rid of my youthful vigor. So I also widened my throat and laughed. However, they didn't seem to expect an old man to have such an attitude. The second firecracker was used on a young woman. After running for a while, this behavior was everywhere. It really deserves to be called the New Year's atmosphere on the first day of the New Year. If I didn't have this bit of old energy, I might have bought a few to have fun; however, I was too embarrassed, so I just stood next to a stall and watched coldly. As long as they laughed, I laughed along with them. Isn't that the most economical way? The policeman standing in the middle of the road, I know that he also has an childlike innocence. Watching the frightened woman's face lose color, he opened his Shandong big mouth and laughed triumphantly. Naturally, today is the day of amnesty for rickshaw pullers. You can cross the road without following the rules, and turning small turns is even okay. The police officer does not have his usual slow-paced face. He ran to the stall and grabbed a few firecrackers to joke with the young women. The recipients seemed to have no courage to scold "damn you." The police officer is now a street hero, and of course there is no possibility of criticizing the hero's behavior! I don't know how many more first days of the New Year I can spend, but participating in this grand firecracker throwing ceremony every year is also a way to prolong life!

Father

— Xiren

My father died when I was six years old. My image of my father is so vague. Although I can recognize my father's appearance in the portrait, he is young and has no beard. When we children learned to be like adults, we would always touch our upper lip and cough dryly, thinking that being an adult should be like that. This kind of child's psychology continued until I grew up.

After being away from my hometown for three years, my father is still so young and has no beard. But my father's son is already very old. When I touched my beard, my fingers felt a slight stinging pain. I remembered what my grandmother said when I got married: "Poor people have no money, but passing on the family line is the same. You should also have a son to make me happy." So the old lady borrowed money to marry me off. Now I am also going to be a father, and the old lady is indeed happy. I looked at my father's portrait, thinking that the young man gave birth to me and left the world. After I became a father, I don't know how, and I even grew more stinging beards than my father. Every woman hopes that her son will get married sooner and have a grandson for her to hold. Because my father did not live long, my grandmother held me, her grandson, but lost her son, so she hoped to have a great-grandson in me to fill the void. The old lady's love is indelible. When I saw her silver hair, I immediately wanted to go home to serve her, leaving such an old person alone in a broken and too-large empty house. But she wanted me to get married. I drifted to Shanghai for life, and it has been three years. Wrinkles have risen on my forehead, and my beard stings my fingers. Although her grandson is aging so quickly, there will be a child to make her happy. I wrote to tell my wife that she was pregnant, and she wrote to ask my wife to go back, saying that you young people don't know how serious it is, don't force yourself, and don't do too much labor. My aunt and uncle came to Shanghai, and she might come to see me too. Women really like their sons and grandsons, and my wife is also planning what to get for the child; however, I cannot deny that I also like children. My liking for children is because children should make people happy. It is impossible to make a child happy just because I like children. Fathers are not as willing as they are.

I looked at my father's portrait, he is young and has no beard.

Fallen Leaves

— Linian

The more fools there are in the world, the greater the effect of doing things, because only fools can bury themselves in hard work. I hope that inventors will invent an X-ray mirror that can see their own sins.

Marrying a vain wife is the main cause of discord in the family.

After reason overcomes emotion, one feels very great and brave.

The reason why gold is precious is not in itself, but in your psychology.

Material things can only last for a while, while spiritual things can last forever, no matter what.

Sons-in-law and daughters-in-law are both outsiders, but mothers-in-law mostly love their sons-in-law, while mothers-in-law always hate their daughters-in-law.

Luck is a blind person. He doesn't know you, but he will sometimes grope for you.

The greatest loss is the loss of reputation in exchange for benefits.

People who like to chat must be more skilled at lying than anyone else.

A pair of hands cannot resist a few mouths: a pen cannot write all the words.

Standing in front of the light, although it feels bright in front of you, there is a shadow behind you, so fortune and misfortune are always connected.

Don't look down on the ragged beggars as despicable. You should know that their previous lives may have been more comfortable than your current life.

The profession of a night soil collector is extremely noble, serving the public on the one hand and earning a living for oneself on the other.

Those who are humble like an empty valley are the hardest to fathom their talents, knowledge, and everything else.

If you close the door and beat the dog, the dog will fight you desperately. If you heat the soup and kill the pig, the pig will howl wildly a few times. If you walk into a desperate situation and are willing to sink without struggling, you are not as good as a dog or a pig.

Street Scene

— Dao

Walking from Sapporo Road, someone followed behind, shouting, "Sir, sir!" Looking back, it turned out to be a gray-uniformed soldier. I stopped and looked at him. He said sincerely, "Sir, may I ask which way to go to Longhua?" He was asking for directions. "Go straight ahead, out of the concession, and ask someone again. It's a long way." After I answered, I was about to walk away, but the man bowed and said with a smile, "Sir, I was dismissed from the army. I don't have the money to go home. Can you help me?" Asking for money! My heart was stunned. He continued, "I was originally a farmer at home, and then I became a soldier. Farmers want to be proud... Sir, you know, now I don't have the money to go home." I had something to do and couldn't wait for him to say more, so I gave him a few copper coins and went my way. He was still following behind, "Sir, give me more. I don't ask people for money casually." I gave him a few more copper coins, "That's enough, that's enough. I'm also a poor man without money. Go ask someone else." Saying that, I hurried away, and he turned to beg another person. Only then did I feel relieved. Unexpectedly, I had just slowed down when I heard, "Sir, I have no food to eat, give me two copper coins." It was a poor woman, holding a baby in her arms. I thought I wasn't a sir and could ignore it, so I went my way. Unexpectedly, a child followed, still shouting, "Sir, I have no food to eat..." To save trouble, I gave him two copper coins. The child saw a lady walking across the road. Ignoring the car's warning, he ran across the road in front of the car. I couldn't help but stop and shout, "Car, don't go!" But it was too late. The car stopped with a screech, and the driver cursed, "Little pig!" Sitting in the car was a noble lady and a small baby. Seeing this contrasting situation of mother and child of different wealth and poverty, a small wave rose in my heart, and this wave made my heart a little uneasy. However, I had something to do, so I went my way.
